1b1(rgyug): rgya gar skad du
2a1(rgyud): / Ar+ya many+dzu shrI na ma sang gi ti/ bod skad du/ 'phags pa
2a2(rgyud): 'jam dpal gyi mtshan yang dag por brjod pa/ 'phags pa 'jam dpal gzhon
2a3(rgyud): nur gyur pa la phyag 'tshal lo// de nus dpal ldan rdo rje 'chang // gdul dka
2a4(rgyud): 'dul ba rnams kyi mchog/ dpa' bo 'jig rten gsum las rgyal// rdo rje dbang phyug
2a5(rgyud): gas rgyu la// pad+ma ma kAr po rgyas pang+gA'i sman// pad+ma myu r+g+ha skye 'dra'i nam+bu mnga'
2b1(rgyud): rang gi lag rdo rje mchog/ yang dang yang du gsor byed pakhre gnyer rim par ldan la sogs// lag na rdo rje
2b2(rgyud): mtha' yas pa// dpa' bo gdul dka' 'dul ba po// 'jigs su rung dang dpa' byed cen// rdo rje rtse mo rab
2b3(rgyud): 'phro ba/ rang gi lag gis gsor byed pa// snying rje che dang shes rab dang // thabs kyis 'gro don byed pa'i
2b4(rgyud): mchogaso dga' mgu rangs pa'i bsam pa tsan/ khro bo'i lus kyi gzugs ldan pa// sangs rgyas
2b5(rgyud): 'phrin las byed pa'i mgon// lus btud rnams dang ldan gcig tu// de bzhin gshegs pa bcom ldan
2b6(rgyud): 'dasardzogs sangs rgyas la phyag 'tshal nas// thal mo sbyar ba byas nas ni// sman sngar 'dug nas

3a2(rgyud): bcu'i phyir// sgyu 'phrul dra bas mngon rdzogs pa'i// byang chub ci nas bdag thob mdzod// nyon mongs pas ni
3a3(rgyud): sems dkrugs shing // mi shes 'dam du bying ba yi// sems can kun la sman pa dang // bla med 'bras bu
3a4(rgyud): thob bya'i phyir// rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das// 'gro ba'i bla ma ston pa po// dam tshig chen
3a5(rgyud): po de nyid mkhyen// dbang po bsam pa mkhyen/ mchog gi// bcom ldan 'das kyi ye shes sku// gtsug gto
3a6(rgyud): chen po tshig go bdag/ ye shes sku ste rang byung ba// 'jam dpal ye shes sems dpa' mo// ming ni ya

3b4(rgyud): rnams kyi dga' bzhin du// glur blangs gang legs pa shad du gsol// mgon po rdzogs sangs rgyas kun gyi// gas
3b5(rgyud): 'dzin ci nas bdag 'gyur phyir// nges par 'byung ba'i bar du 'di// bdag gi bsam pa brtan pos gzung

4b2(rgyud): dang rdzogasang stegs rig sngags 'chang ba'i rigs// rigs gsum la ni rnam par gzigs/ 'jig rten 'jig rten 'das pa'i rigs// 'jig rten
4b3(rgyud): snang byed rigs chen dang // phyag rgya chen po'i rigs mchog dang // rigs chen gtsug gtor chen gzigs nas// tshig gi bdag pos tshigs su

5a1(rgyud): mchod pa chen po zhe sdang che// nyon mongs kun gyi dgra che ba// mchod pa chen po gti mug che// gti mug blo ste gti mug sel// mchod pa chen po
5a2(rgyud): ba che khro ba chen po dgra che ba// mchod pa chen po chags pa che// chags pa thams cad sel bar byed// mchod pa chen po te de ba che// dga' ba chen po mgu ba che// gzugs
5a3(rgyud): chetshe lus kyang che ba ste// kha dog che zhing lus bong che// ming yang che zhing rgya che ba// dkyil 'khor chen po yangs pa yin// shes rab mtshon chen 'chang ba ste// nyon mongs chen po
5a4(rgyud): lcags kyu mchog// grags chen snyan grags chen po ste// snang ba chen po gsal ba che// mkhas pa sgyu 'phrul chen po 'chang // sgyu 'phrul chen po'i don grub pa/ 
5a5(rgyud): sgyu 'phrul chen po dga' bas dga'// sgyu 'phrul chen po'i mig 'phrul can// smin bdag chen po gtsobo ste// tshul khrims chen po 'chang ba'i mchog/ bzod chen 'chang ba
5a6(rgyud): brtan pa po/ brtson 'grus chen po brtul ba yin// bsam gtan chen po'i ting 'dzin gnas// shes rab chen po'i lus 'chang ba// stobs po che la thabs che ba/ 
5a7(rgyud): smon lam ye shes rgya mtsho ste// byams chen rang bzhin dpag tu med// snying rje chen po blo yi mchog/ shes rab chen po blo chen ldan// mkhas pa chen po thabs che ba// 
5a8(rgyud): 'phrul chen po'i stobs dang ldan// shugs chen mgyogs pa chen po ste// rdzu 'phrul chen po cher grags pa// stobs chen pha rol gnon pa po// srid pa'i ri bo chen
5b1(rgyud): po 'joms// mkhregs shing rdo rje chen po 'cha drag po chen po drag shul tshe// 'jigs tshon 'jigs par byed pa po// mgon po rig mchog chen po ste/ 
5b2(rgyud): ma gsang sngags che ba'i mchog/ theg pa chen po'i tshul la gnas// theg pa chen po'i tshul gyi mchog/ sangs rgyas rnam par snang mdzad che// thub pa
5b3(rgyud): chen po thub chen ldan// gsang sngags tshul chen las byung ba// gsang sngags tshul chen bdag nyid can// pha rol phyin bcu thob pa ste// pha rol phyin pa bcu la
5b4(rgyud): gnasapha rol phyin bcu dag pa ste// pha rol phyin pa bcu'i tshul// mgon po sa bcu'i dbang phyug ste// sa bcu la ni gnas pa po// shes bcu rnam dag
5b5(rgyud): bdag nyid can// shes bcu rnam dag 'chang ba po// rnam pa bcu po don bcu'i don// thub dbang stobs bcu khyab pa'i bdag/ kun gyi don ni ma lus byed/ 
5b6(rgyud): bcu'i dbang ldan che ba po// thog ma med pa spros med bdag/ de bzhin nyid bdag dag pa'i bdag/ bden par smra zhing tshig mi 'gyur// ji skad smras pa de bzhin
5b7(rgyud): byed/ gnyis su med dang gnyis med ston// yang dag mtha' la rnam par gnas// bdag med seng ge'i sgra dang ldan// mu stegs ri dgas ngan 'jigs byed/ 
5b8(rgyud): kun du 'gro ba'i don yod stobs// de bzhin gshegs pa'i yid ltar mgyogs// rgyal ba dgra rgyal rnam par rgyal// 'khor los bsgyur ba'i stobs po
6a1(rgyud): tshogs kyi slob dpon tshogs kyi mchog/ tshogs je tshogs bdag dbang dang ldan// mthu chen gces par 'dzin pa ste// tshul chen gzhan gyi dring mi 'jog
6a2(rgyud): tshig rje tshig bdag smra mkhas pa// tshig la dbang 'tshig mtha' yas// tshig bden pa dang bden pa smra// bden pa bzhi ni ston pa po// phyir mi ldog pa phyir mi 'ong // 'dren pa rang
6a3(rgyud): rgyal bser ru'i tshul// ngos 'byung sna tshogs las byung ba// 'byung ba chen po rgyu cig po// dge slong dgra bcom zags pa zad// 'dod chags bral ba dbang po thul// bde ba rnyed
6a4(rgyud): pa 'jigs med thob// bsil bar gyur pa rnyog pa med// rig pa dang ni rkang par ldan// bde gshegs 'jig rten rig pa'i mchog/ bdag girami 'dzin ngar mi 'dzin
6a5(rgyud): bden pa gnyis kyi tshul la gnas// 'khor ba'i pha rol mthar son pa// bya ba byas pas skam sor gnas// shes pa 'ba' zhig nges gsal ba// shes rab mtshon chas
6a6(rgyud): rnams 'joms pa/ sho ra cho chos rgA la zhesal bar khAn/ zhe 'jig rten snang bar byed pa'i mchog/ chos kyi dbang phyug choso+o kyi rgyu la/ galogs pa'i lam ni ston pa / 
6a7(rgyud): don grub bsam pa grub pa ste// kun tu rtog pa thams cad spangs// rnam par mi rtog dbyings mi zad// chos dbyings dam pa zad mi shes// bsod nams ldan pa bsod
6a8(rgyud): nams tshogs// ye shes ye shes 'byung gnas che// ye shes ldan pa yod med shes// tshogs gnyis tshogs ni bsags pa po// rtag par kun rgyu la rnal 'byor can// 
6b1(rgyud): bsam gtan bsam bya blo ldan bdag/ so so rang rig mi g.yo ba// mchog gi dang po sku gsum 'tshong // sangs rgyas sku lnga'i bdag nyid can// khyab bdag ye shes lnga'i bdag/ sangs
6b2(rgyud): rgyas lnga bdag cod pan can// sman snga chags pa med pa 'dang // sangs rgyas thams cad bskyod pa po// sangs rgyas sras po dam pa mchog/ shes pas srid 'byung skye gnas med/ 
6b3(rgyud): chos las byung ba srid pa sal// gcig pus mkhregs rdo rje'i ba dag/ skyes ma thag tu 'gro ba'i bdag/ nam mkha' las byung rang byung ba// shes rab ye shes me bo che// 
6b4(rgyud): rnam par snang bar byed// ye shes snang ba lam me ba// 'gro d+ha'i sanA me ye shes sgron// gzi brjid chen po 'od gsal ba// sngags mchog mnga' bdag rig sngags rgyal// gsang sngags rgyu la
6b5(rgyud): don chen byed// gtsug gtor chen po rmad byung gtsug/ nam mkha'i bdag po sna tshogs ston// sangs rgyas kun bdag dngos po mchog/ 'gro kun dga' ba'i mig dang ldan// sna tshogs
6b6(rgyud): gzugs can skyed pa po// mchod cing brjod pa drang srong che// rigs gsum 'chang ba gsang sngags 'chang // dam tshig chen po gsang sngags 'dzin// gtso bo dkon mchog gsum mdzin
6b7(rgyud): pa/ theg pa mchog gsum ston pa po// don yod zhags pa rnam par rgyal// 'dzin pa chen po rdo rje zhags// rdo rje lcags kyu zhags pa che// rdo rje 'jigs byed 'jigs par byed/

7a1(rgyud): can 'jogs byes/ rdo rje rnam pa rdo rje stod/ sgyu 'grus 'ordo gsum than// rdo rje las rgyas rdo rje'i na rnga'i stong pa mkha' 'jug// po g.yo rol po gtsun
7a2(rgyud): bskyes/ brang can gyi rnon gros su phyin// drag chen ha tu zhes stogs zhes sngags phyogs par byed// gang po chen po yang rgya mthun/ rdo rje gang por sgrog su la/ rdorna
7a3(rgyud): 'chang rdo rje can// rdo rje gcig pu g.yul sel ba// rdo rje 'bar ba mig mi pa dang // sgra yang rdo rje 'bar ba ste// rdo rje 'bebs pa 'bebs pa che// mig brgya pa ste rdo rje'i mig/ 
7a4(rgyud): nA rdo rje'i ba spu can// rdo rje'i su ni gcig pu'i lus// sen mo skyes pa rdo rje'i phyo/ rdo rje'i snying pa pags pa 'khrigs// rdo rje'i sgong thogs dpal du ldan/ rdo rje rgyan gyis byargya
7a5(rgyud): gad rgyangs hata nges par sgrogs// yi ge drug pa rdo rje'i sgra// 'jam dbyangs chen po smran pa// 'jig rten gsum na sgra gcig pa/ nam mkha'i mtha' la m+b+ha sgrogs pa// sgra

9a1(rgyud): rig sngags rgyal// rdo rje rnon po ral gri che/ yi ge mchog ste rnam par dag// theg pa chen po sdug bsngal gcod// mtshon cha chen po rdo rje chos// rdo rje zang
9a2(rgyud): 'dzin na 'jig/ rdo rje blo gros don bzhin na// pha rol phyin pa kun rdzogs pa// sa rnams kun gyi rgyun dang ldan// rnam par dag po bdag med chos// yang dag ye shes zla 'ong bang
9a3(rgyud): brtson chen sgyu 'phrul dra ba ste// rgyud kun gyi ni bdag po mchog// rdo rje'i bdan ni ma lus ldan// ye shes sku rnams ma lus 'chang // kun du bzang po blo gros bzang // sa yi snying po 'gro ba 'a
9a4(rgyud): sangs rgyas kun gyi snying po che// sprul pa'i 'khor lo sna tshogs 'chang // som kyi sa na cho// ma du rgya mas// skye med chos te sna tshogs don// chos kun ngo bo nyid 'chang ba// shes rab chen

9a7(rgyud): sems can thams cad rab grol byed// nyon mongs g.yul du gcig dpa' ba// mi shes dgra yi dregs pa 'joms// blo ldan sgeg 'ching dpal dang ldan// brtan po mo sdug
9a8(rgyud): gzugs 'chang ba// lag pa brgya po kun bskyod cing // gom pa'i stabs kyis gar byed pa// dpal ldan lag pa brgyas gang la// nam mkha' khyab por gar byed pa/ sa'i dkyil
9b1(rgyud): 'khor bzhi yi khyon// rkang pa ya gcig mthil gyis gnon// rkang 'theb sen me'i khyen gyis kyang // tshangs pa'i yul sa rtse nas gnon// don gcig gnyis med chos kyi don// dam pa'i don te
9b2(rgyud): 'jigs pa med// rnam rig sna tshogs gzugs don can// sems dang rnam shes rgyud dang ldan// dngos don ma lus rnams la dga'// stong pa nyid dga' 'dod chags blo// srid pa'i 'dod chags
9b3(rgyud): segs spangs pa// srid gsum dga' ba chen po pa// sprin dkar dag pa bzhin du dkar// 'od bzang ston ka'i zla ba'i 'od// nyi ma 'char ka'i dkyil ltar mdzes// sen mo'i 'od ni shas cher dmar/ 
9b4(rgyud): cod pan bzang po mthon ka'i rtse// skra mchog mthon ka chen po can// nor bu chen po 'od chags dpal// sangs rgyas sprul pa'i rgyal dang ldan// 'jig rten khams brgya kun bskyod cing //

9b6(rgyud): brgyad tshul rig/ yang dag sangs rgyas lam rig pa// sems can kun la shas cher chags// nam mkha' lta bur chags pa med// sems can kun gyi yid la 'jug/ sems can kun gyi yid
9b7(rgyud): ltar 'gyogs// sems can kun gyi dbang don shes// sems can kun gyi yid 'phrog pa// phung po lnga don de nyid shes// rnam dag phung po lnga 'chang ba// nges 'byung kun gyi mtha' la gnas/ 
9b8(rgyud): nges par 'byung ba kun la mkhas// nges 'byung kun gyi lam la gnas// nges par 'byung ba kun ston pa// yan lag bcu gnyis srid rtsa ston// dag pa rnam pa bcu gnyis 'chang // bden
10a1(rgyud): byazhi'i tshul gyi rnam pa can// shes pa brgyad po rtogs po 'arnyed // bden don rnam pa bcu gnyis ldan// de nyid rnam pa bcu drug rig/ rnam pa nyi shu byang chub pa// rnam
10a2(rgyud): ngas rgyas zhan rig mchog/ 6sangs rgyas kun gyi sprul pa'i skra// bre ba dpag med 'gyed pa po/ skad cig thams cad mngon par rtogs// sems kyi skad cig don kun rig/ theg pa sna tsho/ 
10a3(rgyud): thabs tshul gyis// 'gro ba'i don ni rtogs pa po// theg pa gsum gyis nges 'byung la// theg pa gcig gi 'bras bur gnas// nyon mongs khams rnam dag pa'i bdag/ las kyi khams
10a4(rgyud): rnams zad byed pa// chu bo rgya mtsho kun las rgal// spob pa'i dgon pa las byung ba// nyon mongs nye ba kun nyon mongs// bag chags bcas pa gtan spangs pa// snying rje chen po shes rab thabs// 
10a5(rgyud): don yad 'gro ba'i don byed pa/ 'ju nas kun gyi don spongs shing // rnam shes don ni 'gag par byed// sems can kun yid yul dang ldan// sems can kun gyi yid rig pa// sems can kun

10a8(rgyud): rgyasaH/ sangs rgyas kun gyi rang bzhin 'chang // lus med lus te lus kyi mchog/ lus kyi mtha' ni rtogs pa po// gzugs rnams sna tshogs kun du ston/ nor bu chen
10b1(rgyud): rin tshan tog// sangs rgyas kun gyi rtogs bya ba// sangs rgyas byang chub bla na med// gsang sngags las byung yi ge med// gsang sngags chen po rigs gsum pa// gsang sngags don kun bskyed
10b2(rgyud): pa po/ thig le chen po yi ge med// stong pa chen po yi ge lnga// thig le stong pa yi ge brgya// rnam pa kun ldan rnam pa med// bcu drug phyed phyed thig le can// yan lag med pa'i brtsis las 'ang/

10b6(rgyud): chas pa ste// snying rje yi ni ya lang bgos// shos rab ral gri mda' gzhu thogs// nyon mongs mi shes g.yul ngo sel// dpa' bo bdud dgra bdud thub pa// bdud bzhi'i 'jigs pa sel bar byed
10b7(rgyud): bdud kyi dpung rnams pham byed pa// rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas 'jig rten 'dren// mchod 'os bstod 'os phyag gi gnas// rtag tu ri mor bya ba'i 'os// bkur 'os brjod par bya ba'i mchog/ 
10b8(rgyud): phyag byar 'os pa bla ma'i rab/ 'jig rten gsum po gom cig bgrod// mkha' ltar mtha' med rnam par gnon// gsum rig gtsang mar dag pa ste// mngon shes drug ldan rjes dran drug/ 
11a1(rgyud): byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' che// rdzu 'phrul chen po'i jig rten 'das// shes rab pha rol phyin pa'i mtha'// shes rab kyis ni de nyid thob// bdag rig gzhan
11a2(rgyud): rig thams cad pa/ kun la phan pa'i gang zag mchog/ dper bya kun las 'das pa ste// shes dang shes pa'i bdag po mchog/ gtso bo chos kyi sprin bdag ste// phyag rgyo bzhi po'i don
11a3(rgyud): ston pa/ 'gro ba'i bsnyen bkur gnas kyi mchog/ nges 'byung gsum po bgrod rnams kyis// don gyi dam pa rnam dag dpal// 'jig rten gsum na skal bzang che// dpal ldan 'byor
11a4(rgyud): pa kun byed pa// 'jam dpal dpol dang ldan pa'i mchog/ mchog sbyin rdo rje mchog khyod 'dud// yang dag mthar gyur khyod la 'dud// stong nyid lus byung khyod la 'dud// sangs
11a5(rgyud): rgyas byang chub khyod la 'dud// sangs rgyas chags pa khyod la 'dud// sangs rgyas 'dod la phyag 'tshal 'dud// sangs rgyas dgyes po khyod la 'dud// sangs rgyas rol la phyag 'tshal
11a6(rgyud): sangs rgyas 'dzum pa khyod la 'dud// sangs rgyas bzhed la phyag 'tshal 'dud// sangs rgyas gsung nyid khyod la 'dud// sangs rgyas thugs la phyag 'tshal 'dud// med pa las
11a7(rgyud): byung khyod la 'dud// sangs rgyas 'byung ba khyod bdud// nam mkha' las byung khyed la 'dud// ye shes las byung khyod la 'dud// sgyu 'phrul dra ba khyod la 'dud// sangs rgyas rol ston
11a8(rgyud): khyod la 'dud// thams cad thams cad khyod la 'dud// ye shes sku nyid khyod la 'dud// // lag na rdo rje rdo rje 'chang // 'di ni bcom ldan 'das kyi ye shes kyi sku// de bzhin
11b1(rgyud): gshegs pa thams cad kyi ye shes kyi sku// 'jam dpal ye shes sems dpa'i yongs su dag pa thun mang ma yin pa'i ming yang dag par brjod pa yin te/ khyod kyis dga' ba dang / dang ba dang / mgu ba chen
11b2(rgyud): po bla na med pa skyed pa dang / lus dang ngag dang yid kyi gsang ba yongs su dag par bya ba dang / yongs su ma rdzogs pa dang / yongs su ma dag pa'i sa dang / pha rol du phyin pa dang / bsod nams dang / 
11b3(rgyud): ye shes kyi tshogs rnams yongs su rdzogs shing yongs su dag par bya ba dang / bla na med pa'i don ma rtogs pa rtogs par bya ba dang / ma thob pa thob par bya ba nas/ ji srid du de bzhin gshegs pa

11b5(rgyud): ni rdo rje rdo rje 'chang / 'di ni ngas khyod kyi rgyud la yang gsang sngags thams cad kyi chos nyid kyi byin gyi brlabs kyis byin gyis brlabs so// / lag na rdo rje rje rje 'cha po / gzhan yang ming
11b6(rgyud): dag par brjod pa 'di ni/ thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes dang / sku dang gsung dang thugs kyi gsang ba shin du yongs su dag cing yongs su byang ba'o// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sangs
11b7(rgyud): rgyas byang chub bo// yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rnams kyi mngon par rtogs pa'o// bde bar gshegs pa rnams kyi de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi chos kyi dbyings bla na med pa
11b8(rgyud): thugs su chud pa'o// rgyal ba rnams kyi bdud kyi stobs thams cad pham par mdzad pa'o// stobs bcu dang ldan pa thams cad kyi stobs bcu'i stobs nyid do// thams cad mkhyen pa rnams kyi
12a1(rgyud): thams cad mkhyen pa nyid do// chos thams cad kyi lung ngo // sangs rgyas thams cad kyi yang dag par sgrub pa'o// byang chub sems dpa' chen po thams cad kyi bsod
12a2(rgyud): nams dang / ye shes kyi tshogs yongs su rdzogs pa dri med cing shin tu rnam par dag pa'i skye gnas so// nyan thos dang / rang sangs rgyas thams cad kyi zhing ngo // lha dang mi thams cad
12a3(rgyud): phun sum tshogs pa'o// theg pa chen po'i gzhi'o// byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa rnams kyi 'byung khungs so// 'phags pa'i lam thams cad kyi mtha'o// rnam par grol ba rnam
12a4(rgyud): brtag pa'o// nges par 'byung ba'i lam skye ba'i gnas so// de bzhin gshegs pa'i gdung mi 'chad pa'o// byang chub sems dpa' chen po'i rigs dang rgyud rab tu 'phel ba'o// pha rol

12a6(rgyud): par bsdud pa'o// nges par 'byung ba bgrod pa thams cad kyi 'phags pa'i lam yongs su smin pa'o// tshangs pa'i gnas bzhi la gnas pa rnams kyi ting nge 'dzin to// sems rtse gci

12a8(rgyud): thams cad spong ba'o// sgrib pa thams cad nye bar zhi ba'o// 'ching ba thams cad las rnam par grol ba'o// rdzas thams cad las thar pa'o// sems kyi g.yeng ba thams cad zhi nga'o//

14a1(rgyud): cad brjod du med pa'i rang bzhin nyid do// / lag na rdo rje rdo rje 'chad// gzhan yang rig kyi kyi rigs kyi bu mo gsang sngags kyi sgo'i spyad pa spyod pa gang la las/

14a4(rgyud): 'chang ba dang / klog pa dang / kun chub par byed pa dang / tshul bzhin du yid la byed pa dang / gzhan dag la yang dam tshig bzhin du ji lta ba bzhin du ston pa dang / ming gi don gang yang rung ba

15b1(rgyud): ba'i dbang gi phyir/ ring po mi thogs par de nyid kyi sprul pa'i gzugs kyi lus mthong bar 'gyur ro// sangs rgyas dang byang chub sems dpa' thams cad kyi gzugs kyi sku rnam pa sna tshogs dang ldan pa rnam

15b3(rgyud): mthu 'khob du skye bar mi 'gyur ro// dbang po sa tshang bar mi 'gyur ro// dbang po nyams par mi 'gyur ro// log par lta ba dang / lta ba ngan pa'i rigs su skye bar mi 'gyur ro// sangs rgyas mi bcu
15b4(rgyud): pa'i sangs rgyas kyi zhing du skye bar mi 'gyur ro// sangs rgyas bzhugs na yang des bstan pa'i chos spong ba dang skol bar mi 'gyur ro// lha tshe rings po'i nang du yang skye bar mi 'gyur ro// mu ge dang / nad dang / 
15b5(rgyud): mtshon gyi bar gyi bskal pa'i nang du yang skye bar mi 'gyur ro// snyigs sa lha'i dus su yang skye bar mi 'gyur ro// rgyal po dang / dgra dang / chom rkun gyi 'jigs pa yang 'byung bar mi 'gyur ro// jis
15b6(rgyud): kyang dman pa dang / dbul ba'i 'jigs pa yang 'byung bar mi 'gyur ro// dri ngas dang / skur ba dang / smad pa dang / mi snyan pa dang / gtam ngan gyi 'jigs pa yang 'byung bar mi 'gyur ro// rgyud dang / 
15b7(rgyud): rus dang / rigs bzang po dang yang ldan par 'gyur ro// kun nas mdzes pa dang / gzugs dang / kha dog dang ldan par yang 'gyur ro// 'jig rten pa rnams la sdug pa dang yid du 'ong ba dang / 
15b8(rgyud): 'grogs na bde ba dang / mthong na dga' bar yang 'gyur ro// 'jig rten pa rnams la mdzes pa dang / skal pa dang ldan pa dang tshig brtsan par yang 'gyur ro// gang dang gang du skyes pa de dang der yang
16a1(rgyud): ngangs drang po gyu// mang spong na da / 'thong song bdan yang srud kyo gan mo dang pa dang / 'khor ma thong ba yod 'gyur ro// masus can nyams
16a2(rgyud): mchog dang / yon tan mchog dang ldan par 'gyur ro// rung bzhin gyis kyang pha rol tu phyin pa drug gi yon tan dang ldan par 'gyur ro// tshangs pa'i gnas bzhi la yang gnas par 'gyur ro// dran pa
16a3(rgyud): dang shes bzhin dang / thangs dang stongs dang / smon lam dang / ye shes dang ldan par yang 'gyur ro// bstan chos thams cad las 'jigs pa med pa dang / snga mkhas par yang 'gyur ro// 
16a4(rgyud): pab dang / tshig gsal ba dang / sgren por yang 'gyur ro// shes nyen can dang / le lo med pa dang / chog shes pa dang / nor mang ba dang / sred pa med par yang 'gyur ro// sems can thams cad kyis
16a5(rgyud): mchog tu yid brtan par bya ba dang / slob dpon dang bla mar bkur bar yang 'gyur ro// des sngon ma thos pa'i bzo dang / sgyu rtsal dang / mngon par shes pa'i shes pa dang / bstan chos thams cad kya
16a6(rgyud): don dang /  yi ge'i sgo nas shes par 'gyur ro// tshul khrims dang 'tsho ba dang kun du spyod pa shin du yongs su dag par spyad pa dang / legs par byung ba dang / rla legs par bsnyen pa rdzogs par 'gyuraro// 
16a7(rgyud): thams cad ga khyen pa nyid kyi byang chub kyi sems kyang mi brjed par 'gyur ro// nyan thos ring dgra bcom pa dang rang sangs rgyas kyi nges po la nam yang 'jug par mi 'gyuraro// // lag na rdza
16a8(rgyud): de ltar yon tan dpag tu med pa dag dang ldan par 'gyur te/ rnam pa de lta bu'i yon tan gyi tshogs dpag tu med pa gzhan dag dang yang ldan par 'gyur ro// // lag na rdo rje rdo rje 'chang // don dam
16b1(rgyud): po'i mdo yang dag par rjod pa 'di yang dag par 'dzin pa'i skyes du gang zag de ni bsod nams dang ye shes kyi tshogs legs par bsags shing / sangs rgyas kyi yo tan rnams shin du myur
16b2(rgyud): bsgrubs nas/ ring po mi thogs par bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub mngon par rdzogs par 'tshong rgya bar 'gyur te/ bskal pa mang por yongs su mya ngan las 'da' ba'i chos su mi 'gyur
16b3(rgyud): par/ sems can thams cad la bla na med pa'i chos ston pa dang / phyogs bcur dam pa'i chos kyi rnga sgra chen po rgyun mi 'chad par sgrogs pa'i chos kyi rgyal po chen por 'gyur ro//

17a1(rgyud): rnam dag legs pa'i lam// zab cing yangs la rgya che ste// don chen 'gro ba'i don byed pa// sangs rgyas rnams kyi yul 'di ni// rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas
17a2(rgyud): kun gyis byA shad/ bcom ldan 'das 'jam dpal ye shes sems dpa'i don dam pa'i mtshan yang dag par brjod pa// bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa shAkya thub pas gsungs pa rdzog
17a3(rgyud): rgya gar skad du/ shrI kA la tsag la glu tan tra rA dz+nyA nA ma/ bod skad du/ dpal dus kyi 'khyer lo'-i'i bsdus pa'i rgyud kyi rgyal po zhes bya'o// 'jam

17a6(rgyud): mam sngon rnaMm kyi mkhom ma marnam 'byor gyi rnams rnam pa' sa snang ba dang blo shes srog la rdo rje ba tsug 'dzin snangs rgyas skad ba sbyin dam sa dang/ blar ma
17b1(rgyud): dang mchog gi drang srong rigs kyi mya ngan 'das pa la sog pa'i// 'dzin pa'i mthar thug khyod kyis zhus pa de mi shes pas tshig gi gnas ldan lus dbus ma lus pa// dkyil 'khor dag ni
17b2(rgyud): dbang dag rnal 'byor pa yis rnam par bshad par bya yis mi bdog shin du nyon// dus kyis stong pa rnams las rlung dang me dang chu dngos dang gling dang ro dang rgya mtsho rnams// rgyu skar rnams da
17b3(rgyud): nyi zla skar ma gda' tshogs drang srong rnams dang lha dang 'byung po klu rnams dang // byol song skye ba rnam pa bzhi rnam pa sna tshogs pa dang sa 'og dag la mi dang dmyal ba'i rnams// chu las tsha 'byung ba 'i/ 
17b4(rgyud): du sgo nga las kyang yin te stong pa las ni 'byung ba nyid rnams skyed// sku dang ye shes nam mkha' nges par rlung dang me dang chu dang sa dang brtan dang skye 'gro dang // mi mthong ba'i lha nyid skye ba rnams dang granas ni
17b5(rgyud): rnam pa bcu ru brjod pa rdo rje'i sku// yang dag 'byung ba'i sngags kyi skye gnas yin te 'di nyid slar log pa las 'jig rten mi bdag kye// de ltar gang gi yang dag rig pa de ni phyugs ma yin te sems
17b6(rgyud): kyi rnam rtog grol ba'o// g.yon pa'i yan lag la ni dkar po'i 'od zer skye 'gro'i bdud rtsi'i cha ste g.yas su kha dog dmar// sgro gcan dus me zla nyi zla ba'i bu dang mig dmar dag ste pa ba sangs dang du
17b7(rgyud): 'jug rings spen pa dag dang char dang rdo rje dang ni chu dang me ste bdun zung 'jig rten du// mun pa bral ba'i yod pa'i zung cig mun pa'i mtha' ma rnams la nges par 'od zer 'brar ba rnams// sku
17b8(rgyud): ma rnams zhu dang sa gnyis dbye bas de rnams bzhi ste srog gi ming ni rlung cig la// rnam pa bcu ni steng dang 'og dang shar dang nub kyi phyogs su gnag dang ser ba rnams su 'gyur// dbus su
18a1(rgyud): rdo rje steng du sa bon de nyid nus pa 'og ma yon tan tshegs ldan yang dag gnas// kun gyi stong du stong dang ye shes zhi ba'i tshig ldan dngos rnams thams cad kyis ni rnam pa
18a2(rgyud): grol te a sogs gang zhig tsA yi ra wa lar ldan dbyangs rnams sum bcu de rnams zla ba nyi ma'i cha// kA sogs sde tshan dbyangs dang bcas rnams nyi ma rgyu ba stong pa dang ni drug dang me rnams kyis

18a5(rgyud): sogs gtsug gtor 'khor lo dang ni snying ka mgrin pa mgo dang lte ba'i 'khor lo'i rim pa yis// sna tshogs gnag dang dmar dang ri bong can dang ser rnams kyis ni phung po khams rnams lhag pa'i lha// 
18a6(rgyud): sa lhun po'i dbus la dmyal ba klu'i grong khyer dag la dpag tshad 'bum phrag gnyis// ri rab lhun po 'bum gyi tshang ste gza' tshegs gnas la stong phrag nyi shu rtsa lnga ni// mgrin pa nyid
18a7(rgyud): dang gdong la lnga bcu mi g.yo'i gnas la nges par nyi shu rtsa lnga de bzhin no// de'i phyi rol stong pa cig pu srid pa gsum bral yon tan med pa de nyid dman pa'o// rlung gi mtha' nas rlung gi mtshams

18b1(rgyud): blo la ni nyi khyim 'khor lo bskor mar bcas pa nyin mtshan 'khor// phyogs rnams drug du 'bum phrag gnyis gnyis srid pa gsum po mtha' dag dus sbyor las ni rab tu skyes/ 'jig rten khas
18b2(rgyud): rnams ma lus kun la zheng la sum 'gyur mtha' skor rnams kyi tshad la yin pa las// sa'i mtha' skor la ni 'bum phrag gsum ste chu sa la rlung la drug dgu nyi rnams rim pa yis// gang
18b3(rgyud): zhig phyi rol du ni srid gsum gnas la dpag tshad 'bum phrag gcig ste lus pa nyid la yang / khru gang pa ste sa stengs gnas pa rnams la rang rang tshad ni yang dag yin te mi dbang kye/ 
18b4(rgyud): rdul phran brgyad kyis phra mo gcig ste phra mo 'di brgyad kyis ni skra'i rtse mo'i phra mo dang / nyi rdul dang ni shig dang nas dang sor mo'i lto nyid rnams ste sor tshigs nyi ma zung rnams kyis// khru ste
18b5(rgyud): / de bzhi rnams kyi gzhu la 'dir ni gzhu ru gyur pa stong phrag rnam pa gnyis kyis ni// rgyang grags 'gyur ste rgyud byug dun gyi TI len b+h+yas su sa stengs nam mkha'i tshad// dang por chos bzang skal pa zung dang
18b6(rgyud): ldan bzhi ste tshangs pa 'jig rten las ni 'das pa'o// dpal gyi skal pa dkar po'o skal pa shin tu dbang gyur srid pa la gnas 'dod pa bcu gcig ste// gzugs med rnams kyi a la sogs

19a1(rgyud): @/ kaseg ma'i chu ru nges par brjod pa'i dmyal pa'i bye ma'i chu gnyis pa'o// 'dam gyi chu dang bzod rke du ba tsha ba dang yang mun pa dang ni du 'bad bdun pa'o// cha dang chang dang rma/

20b1(rgyud): bas narnyed pa steng du rab tu bcug pa mi'i bdag po zla bya bsdus pa rnam par dag pa'o// gang zhig zla rnams gsum 'gyur ba'i dbu ma'i phung po gnas pa ma bA dang / ni mye y-is bsgyur/

20b3(rgyud): tu bcug par gyur pa thub mchog rnams kyis bgos pa'i lhag ma gza'// gnas gnyis la ni nyi ma zla ngas bsres pa mtshams dang nyi mas bgos pa 'byung bas bsres pa ste// de ni steng gi
20b4(rgyud): phung por sbyin la dang por lag pas bsgyur la bsdus pa brgyad dang gnyis kyis bgo// gnas gsum dbus ma dbang phyug gis bsgyur 'og la dgu dang yon tan rnams kyis thob la gnyis bsres

21a1(rgyud): mchi la byugs// ces zhes bya ba bcu gcigs ste bcudang rgya mtsho'i rkang mar nyi bur gcig gis ma gang ba// lnga dang drug par nyid shu gnyis bye marnams dan
21a2(rgyud): la rgyal ba nyid dang bdun par nyi shu lnga// tshes kyi chu tshed de rnams nyi ma'i rab tu dbye ba rnams kyis sngon dang 'brid par 'gyur ba ste// 'byung dang 'byung ba mnga' dang rig byed me lag ri bong can rnaMm
21a3(rgyud): sngon gyi cha dang gzhan la yang // bsdus pa'i cha la rgya mtsho zla ba rnams kyis mnyam dang mi mnyam song bas rgyu la sman dang 'brid// mtshams dang nyi ma yis ni cha thob pa'i lhag ma yang dag rgyu ba/ 
21a4(rgyud): bzhin bsgyur bar bya// de nyid nyi ma'i dbye ba nyi mo'i rkang pa chu tshod rnams kyis snron dang 'brid par 'gyur ba ste/ ches la rig byed kyis bsgyur de la nor gyis gsal bar 'gyur te de yi gsum gyi ma yis

26b4(rgyud): gang pa sum bcu rtsa drug rnams la leng spod chu tshod rnams ni 'jig rten tshes kyis bsgyur// phyed bcas zla ba chu ched rnams gnyis nyin zhag so sor 'char ba myur 'khyog bdun dang rgyabo du'o// phyed dang bcas pa zla ba'i
26b5(rgyud): bar du de nyid 'char bar 'gyur te mi yi 'jig rten rnams su snang // phyis ni dpal ldan dus kyi 'khor lor rab zhugs de gang la'i long spyod du yang snang ba med// de'i 'char ba'i cha nyid shes na de yi 'char ba dag
26b6(rgyud): gis mtha' yas dus kun shes par 'gyur ba'o// lo yi nyin zhag lnga yis bsgyur la yang ni mnga' yis nges bsgyur bgrod pa'i nyi mas rang dman la// bug pa rnams kyis nges par bsres par 'gyur ba rang
26b7(rgyud): 'gro son tan dbang lam gza' rnams dkyil 'khor te// sa'i bu'i ri ngang klu deng drug rnams nyin nag tshogs su 'gyur te ringang thug pa ra~M ku rnams// rdza skyes kyis skye sa ma'i rig byed lha'i bla mar 'gyur te
26b8(rgyud): sangs kyi ri rgyal mig/ nyi ma'i bu'i drug dang drug ste ri dang nam mkha' gcig gi nyin zhag tshegs rnams dkyil 'khor ro// ri dang mtshams dang gcig rnams skyes bu de ni nor nges yin te zla ba'i bu ru brgyas
27a1(rgyud): bsgyur la/ me gnyis ri yis dman byas pa ba sangs la bcus bsgyur nyi ma rnams las rgya mtsho brgyad dman pa// sngags par stong pa nam mkha' mtsham
27a2(rgyud): dmag yon te nyi skyes mkha' lag gdongs ka dus rnams bu min 'gyur/ nas skyes su ni phyed bcas dgu dang gza' lag byed bcas mi'i bdag po nyi skar bla mar 'gyur// pa ba sangs la drug
27a3(rgyud): bu la sbyin zhes mtha' dag long spyod dbus su sbyong ba'o// de ltar dag pa'ang de rnams mi yi dbang po skye ba'i skar ma rgyu ba'i dbang las gyur pa'o// rang gi yan lag du ni chung ngu'i dag par 'gyur te nyin
27a4(rgyud): dbus che/  gyur pa 'gro dbang la// zla ba drug gis zla ba'i long stod bsgyur bya yin te dus kyi 'khor lo'i lo dang zla ba yis// cha thob long spyod bu lon 'gyur te nyi ma ri bong can gyis long ma spyad pa chu tshong
27a5(rgyud): phyed/ 'jug rings kyi ni slar yang lhag pa gang zhig so so'i nyi dus zla ba'i nyin zhag rnams kyis bsgyur// drug bcu'i cha yis chu tshod rnams ni so so'i nyin zhag du su myur dang 'khyog por 'char ba'o// 
27a6(rgyud): zla skyes sngags pa myur bar rab tu skye ba yin te stobs ldan sa skyes 'jug rings 'khyog por ro// da la dang pa ba sangs dag dal te rang bzhin yon tan dbang gis lhag ma rgyu ba stobs med do// myur la shar
27a7(rgyud): du gdong phyogs yin te yang ni nub tu gdong phyogs 'khyog por rgyu ba rab tu zhugs// dal bar lho ru gdong yin rang gi 'gro ba'i yon tan dbang las nges par 'byung ba byang phyogs 'gyur// zla ba'i nyin
27a8(rgyud): zhug sum bcu rgya mtshos bsgyur na nam mkha' mig dang zla ba zla ba'i rkang pa ste// phung po bcu gnyis rnams la dus kyis bsgyur na brgyad dang rig byed nyi ma rnams kyis rkang pa'o// de yi dbus su 'grib
27b1(rgyud): pa dang ri 'phol ba nyid ni bgrod 'gro'i dbang las mong sa pa yis/ 'khor lo'i phyed dang phyed du klu'i dus tshogs rnams kyis ni ma'i bdag po mtha' dag rig par bya/ mtshams kyis gcad la sgra gcan dkyil
27b2(rgyud): 'khor rab tu 'jug pa ri bong can gyi dkyil 'khor nyid la'o// thams cad rnam par dag par ba drung na ri bong can gyi dbang gis dkyil 'khor drug bcu'i chu chod 'gyur/ byed bzung ba ni byed kyi dag pa yin snga
27b3(rgyud): bong can gyi dbang gis chu tshod yod pa'i bar// nyin mtshan dus su dkar dang gnag la mtshams kyis bcang la nyi ma zla ba 'dzin par 'gyur ba'o// mi rnams kyis ni lo la brgya yis bsgyur bar byas pa'i la mas
27b4(rgyud): gza' rnams kyi ni long spod do// gnas gnyis pa la phyogs kyis cha thob pa yis steng dang phung por bu lon du ni sbyang bar bya/ 'bum phrag nyi shu dang ni gcig dang drug khri rnams kyi lo grangs rnams kyis
27b5(rgyud): dus kyi phyed nyid do// phyis ni khyim gnyis dag gis rab tu yin par 'gyur ba nges par lo'i grangs ldan bzhi rnams so// stong pa dang ni stong pa nam mkha' klu dang lag pa thub pa ri bong can rnams rdzogs
27b6(rgyud): ldan tshad// mkha' dang nam mkha' stong pa dang ni ro dgu nyi ma rnams kyis gsum ldan lo grangs rab tu 'grub// stong pa stong pa mkha' dang rig byed ro dang sbrul zhes pa ni gnyis ldan ro rnams yang dag
27b7(rgyud): snang ba dang ni rnamam pa' ma' jig yon tan rtsom tsho'i rdo blangs rnams kyi pa du lu dus su'igyum mi 'dunams rgyas dus kyimatho'i dug ni tshogs kyi da dmas kyis kyis sa
27b8(rgyud): stong par gnas// tha skar la sogs phyis ni rab tu skye ba zhes pa de bzhin spyid zla 'bring po la sogs dang // gza' dang sbyor ba dang ni tshes dang byed pa la sogs nges par de bzhin gzhan yang de dus
28a1(rgyud): lha rnams dang ji lha ma yin rnams su stengs gnas su drag po'i 'thag mo rab tu 'gyur ba'o// sde tshan drug dang dbyangs rnams bcas pa rnams ni nges par yon tan gyis brgya
28a2(rgyud): lo gsum nyin zhag rnams// a sogs thung ngu la sogs zhes bya ri bong can cha yon tan gsum gyis phyed bcas zla ba'o// gang zhig rtsa rnams hA sogs dbyangs dang bcas pa sumabacu
28a3(rgyud): nyin dang mtshan mo rnams la sgra gcan gyi// dpal ldan stong pa gzhom du med pa la sogs gsum gyis bsgyur ba gang de sgra ga can dus stor te// mi yi bdag po lo gsum phyed bcas zla ba rnams
28a4(rgyud): la 'byung ba nyi ma zla ba'i grangs su 'gyur// byed bcos zla ba dor nas thub pa mchog rnams kyis ni bcad pa dus kyi 'khor lor 'gyur ba'o// zla bar gza' gcig nor yin mi bdag gnyis 'gyur
28a5(rgyud): chu tshod la ste bsdus pa la gnyis rkang pa mda'o// 'khor los rnam par phye bas gza' ru 'gyur te drug bcu rnams la de bzhin sbyin par bya ba ni sum bcu rtsa gnyis rnams kyis chu tshod la ste thub pa
28a6(rgyud): klus bsgyur bsdus pa bya bar gnyis bcas sbyin// bsnon dang 'bring dang bsnan pa ri mong can yin rkang pa lnga dang bcas pa drug po 'di rnams kyis// zla phyed gsum gyi nyin zhag yon tan sum
28a7(rgyud): lngapa du yang 'gyur te long spyod rab tu 'grub// skar ma gnyis la drug bcus bsgyur dung dad pa'i chos kyi nyin zhag dang bcas drag po'i long spod rnams// de ltar dpal ldan dus kyi 'khor lo ga
28a8(rgyud): tshogs ldan pa phyi dang lus rnams su ni tha mi dad// bsdu dang spro ba'i rgyur ni sred pa gsum gyi gnas su dus kyi rang bzhin gyis ni nyi shing tha bas dang shes rabya rab tu da bye bas mnyam dang
28b1(rgyud): mi mnyam rims kyis myur 'khyog la sogs rgyu ba rnams/ 'dod 'chags bral ba rnams dang thub mchog rigs rnams dang ni tshangs grag la sogs lha rnams kyis mi shes// gang zhig a sogs
28b2(rgyud): dbyangs lnga rnams dang dang po'i tshes sogs dbang las dga' ba la sogs lnga rnams sbyor// de rnams 'dir ni 'char bar byed de gal gal te mi'i bdag po sa skyes la sogs gza' rnams dang bral na/ 
28b3(rgyud): sa skyes mi 'dod pa la shar bar nges par gal te gyur na yang ni smin drug ster nyid dang // de ru g.yul dang nad rnams gal te byung na mi rnams 'chi bar 'gyur ba dang po'i dbyangs ljon no// bzong por zla
28b4(rgyud): skyes mchu dag sbyor ba gal te yin na gnyis pa 'chi ba nyid 'dir gza' ru'o// rgyal bar bla ma nyid dang skag dag gal te 'gro ba yin na gsum pa 'chi bar 'gyur ba'o// stong pa'i chos su pa ba sangs
28b5(rgyud): mon gru gal te 'gro ba yin na bzhi pa 'chi bar 'gyur ba'o// gang pa spen pa dang ni bra nyer bcas pa rab tu gyur na lnga pa 'gro ba 'chi ba la// nyi ma dga' bar shwar na dmar yang 'gyur te nad pa rnams ni nyon mongs
28b6(rgyud): nyid du 'gyur ba'o// zla ba bzang por shar ba la yang de bzhin nges par rab tu 'thab mo nad nyid rnams su'o// lnga rnams 'char la bden par yin te 'bras bu mang po 'chi ba'i sbyor ba rnams las rnam
28b7(rgyud): bralashes par bya ba nang dang 'thab mo dge dang mi dge 'a 'bras bu yul nas 'gro dang bag ma yin// de ltar skar ma dang ni gza' rnams dbyangs tshogs chos rnams de nyid lnga'i rab tu dbye ba yis/ 
28b8(rgyud): zla ba phyed dang zla ba 'grong dang lo ru yang ni 'char ba 'dir 'gyur drug bcu'i lo rnams la// snying zla 'bring po la sogs de nyid yan lag bcu gnyis kyis 'char zla ba phyed kyi dbye ba yis// 'du
29a1(rgyud): bcu rtsa gnyis nyi ma rnams kyis 'char ba 'drir ni 'gyur ba zla ba'i dbye bas dbyangs rnams so// zla drug rnams ni bgrod pa'i cha dang rab tu skye ba'i sgor gyur rnams kyis bcu
29a2(rgyud): gnyis lo rnams la// de ltar dbyangs lnga rnams kyis 'char bar 'di ru 'gyur ba dang ni nub pa de ltar phyi nas so// thog mar byis pa'i dbyings ni rlung rang tshes kyi yon tan dbang las dpal ldan
29a3(rgyud): gzhon nu'i gnyis pa ru// long tsho dang ni rgas pa dag rnams rims kyis me dang rgya mtsho'i nyi ma lnga par nub par 'gyur/ a sogs dbyangs lnga rnams la gang zhig nges par yon tan rnams kyis bsgyur
29a4(rgyud): tha gnyis sum bcu nyid de/ kaM sogs sngo tshan yi ge rnams kyi rang bzhin yon tan dbang las mtha' dag rnams kyis sbyor ba'o// thung rgyu rnams ni dkar po'i phyogs la 'char bar 'gyur te de nyid
29a5(rgyud): lnga'i rab tu dbye ba yis// ring po rnams ni nag po'i phyogs la nges par rab tu bskyed dang bsdu ba'i sbyor ba 'gyur ba'o// rgyu skar nyi shu rtsa bdun rnams las nyi ma'i dus spor gsal bar 'di'i chu tshod
29a6(rgyud): rnams ni dga'i cha// de ltar yang ni rang bzhin gsum gnas g.yo dang brtan dang mnyam po lug gi dus sbor la so gras 'dir// lug dang kar ka ta dang srang dang nges par chu srin 'dir ni g.yo ba gnyis
29a7(rgyud): dang brtan pa dang // lhag ma gzhan rnams nyin mtshan dus la bcu gnyis g.yo rang brtan pa gnyis kyi rang bzhin 'char ba'o// de ru yud tsam sum bcu rnams kyang nyin zhag dus la chu chod yang ni drug
29a8(rgyud): bcu tham pa ste// dang po dbyangs rnams sum bcu 'char ba 'dir ni 'gyur ba dang nyid nges par yud tsam yud tsam du// sde tshan sum bcu'i yi ge rnams su 'gyur ba chu tshod thung dang ring po'i rang
29b1(rgyud): tu dbye ba yis// chos kyi cha yis zla ba'i dbus su nges par 'byung ba 'char dang nub pa de ltar de las so// // a sogs dbyangs lnga pa rnams stong pa rlung dang mo dang chu dngo sar gyur
29b2(rgyud): rnams kyis yang dag rigs// sgra gcan dus me zla nyi zla skyes bkra shis pa sangs bla ma ma rungs nyi skyes 'dir lhag lha// sngar gsungs pa'i dus sbyor re rer mtshan mo nyin mo'i dbang las chu tshod
29b3(rgyud): 'di ru bsgrub bya ste// de yis dbus su gang zhig dbyangs 'gyur gza' rnams stobs ldan dkyil 'khor de yis 'dir ni bsgrub bya'o// 'dir ni g.yon du dbyangs rnams thung ngu 'char bar 'gyur te/ 
29b4(rgyud): gzhan yang gnas su dbyangs rnams gzhan ma'o// g.yon du stong pa la sogs de nyid rnams dang gza' tshogs rgyu ba kun gyi gtso bo sgra gcan no// g.yas su sa sogs de nyid rnams dang gza'
29b5(rgyud): tshogs nges par nyi ma'i bu la sogs pa nyid kyis s+ho// phyi'i dus kyi chu tshod dang ni gza'i gnas dang mnyam pa'i dbyangs dang bcas pa nyid rnams bsgrub pa'o// g.yul du brtsod phyir dus me stong pa 'tshor
29b6(rgyud): ba'i// dus dag rnams la dris na 'chi bar rab tu 'gyur// rlung la nyi ma 'pham pa dang ni gzhan yang me las sa skyes dag dang 'char ba rma ru 'gyur ba'o// chu la bla ma grin na 'dum par 'gyur te sa la
29b7(rgyud): spen pa dag 'char brtsod par mi 'gyuraro// 'chi ba dang ni nyon mongs pa dang dmar 'gyur bde dang mnyam rnams 'dri ba po ste nad pa yi// g.yul nyid du ni dgra rnams 'jig par rab tu 'gyur ba
29b8(rgyud): nges par sgra gcan stong par 'char ba dang // rlung du zla ba 'dam par 'gyur dang me la zla ba'i bu nyid 'char na g.yul du rma ru 'gyur// chu ru pa ba sangs kyis nor snyed pa dang sar ni 'jug rings dge 'am
30a1(rgyud): dgra rnams dbang du 'gyur// de ltar ltad mo dang ni bag mar+ya 'bras bu mang por 'gyur te g.yon pa'i lam du gza' rnams kyis// pho nya yis ni smras pa'i dbyangs rnaMs
30a2(rgyud): grang zhig nges par bcus bsgyur ba la khyim gyi 'khor los bsres/ phyis ni 'byung bas bsgyur ba skye bo de nye ba rnams bsnan pa las bdun cha lhag ma rnams// zla bA m+me dang mnga' dang ri rnams mi
30a3(rgyud): mnyam rkang par song bas mi rnams dngos grub med pa ste// mig dang ni byed ro rnams nges par shin du mnyam pa'i rkang par song bas bya ba grub par 'gyur// lo dang zla ba zla ba phyed dang nyin dang mtshan gyi dus
30a4(rgyud): rnams dus sbyor dbusu rab zhugs pa// dus sbyor gcig la lnga'i dbye ba rnams kyis gzo'i tshogs ldan pa dbyangs bcos de nyid dbye ba'o// de nyid gcig la dbugs rnams drug bcu ldog pa'i yo
30a5(rgyud): tan brgya rnams dus kyi chu tshod 'jug par 'gyur// rgya tshong ma rnams la ni chu slang drug bcu rnams t+ye de'i chur 'gyur dbugs drug myi dpyang gro// dbugs 'byung 'jug pa'i dbus su mi dge dge ba'i 'bras
30a6(rgyud): bu shes par 'gyur ba rnal 'byor ldan pa yis// dge dang mi dge shes min chu tshod dus la nyan mtshan 'gro ba'i dbang las bsgrub bya nyid zla dag/ de ltar dus mi shes pa mi dge ba dang dge ba'i 'bra/ 
30a7(rgyud): bu gang dag smra ba 'jig rten 'dir// long pa de yis long ba khrid nas dgon par glang po seng ge dag gis gang bar rab tu zhugs// pu me'i rnal 'byor mi shes pa nyid rnams la bza' stobs ldan pa'i
30a8(rgyud): dus sbyor sbyin pa bya ba nI// dus me nyi ma sa skyes nyi phyed bu rnams skye ba'i dus sbyor btun pa rnams la gnas pa na/ ka'achi be dang ni nad dang rma dang nges par mtha' dag nor 'jig pa yang de la byed pa
30b1(rgyud): yis/ des na de spangs pa yang nges par nga'i tshig gis dus sbyor gzhan las bsngags pa rab tu sbyin/ sgo gcan zla ba zla da'i bu dang bla ma pa sangs skye ba'i dus sbyor bdun pa la gnas na// dgra 'jig
30b2(rgyud): bdag nyid rgya po dang g.yul du rgyal ba zhes bya nor dang bud med bcas par thob par byed// yid dag dus sbyor thams cad kyis ni gal te rang nyid lus kyi g.yon gyi rtsa nas yin pa ni// mtha' dag
30b3(rgyud): sa stengs du ni dag pa'i gza' dang chos kyis nges par don rnams thams cad 'grub par byed// skar ma cha gsum byas pas dgu dang rku dang rku pa rnams kyis skye ba'i skar ma dang po ru// mi rungs pa rna
30b4(rgyud): zla ba dang bcas mi mnyam rkang par song ba 'chi ba nad pa rnams kyi'o// tha skar la sogs rnams kyis rtsa gsum ldan pa sprul bzhin bya ste nam gru'i bar du'o// sdig pa'i zla ba dang ni skye skar gal te rtsa
30b5(rgyud): gcig gyur na mi de rnams ni 'jig pa'o// drug ches brgyad ri zla ba bcu dang dgur banas bcu dang nyi sa nyi shu gcig rnams lo bzangs la/ ny+tsA sa zla ba dgra dang gza' lhag spen pa bla ma k+Sha dang dkar ba
30b6(rgyud): rnams kyi rim pas spong / der ni bye brag gnas skabs dbye bas yang dang yang ste de las mtshan brgya pa yi ge rnams// ma nu s+ya rnams kyis zhi ba ma yin byed ste zhi ba'i ngo bosade par byed pa'i gza' rnaMs
30b7(rgyud): yod dkon 'ab+h+ring bye na mya nig nyi ma chu srin la gnas bum par nyin dgu smra tha chungs dang // 'du byed yin te me bdag nyi ma nyi ma dpyid ma na ma shes nyid ste lug la nyis gnas// dpyid 'bring med
30b8(rgyud): gzugs ste klang Sh+ya TIg b+hur par nyi ga nas dpyid dzA tha tshungs dpar zla bau R+sha ba mo// skye mdzod drug dang reg pa dag ste kar ka Ta dang seng ge nyi gnas gyur pa tshor bsred// dbyar zla 'bring dang tha chungs
31a1(rgyud): na te du mo dang ni srang gnas nyid gyur ston zla 'bring po la// len pa dang ni srid pa rab tu yin te ston zla tha chungs sdig par nyi ma gnas pa la// skye bar 'gyur te gzhu la nyi ma gnas la
31a2(rgyud): rga shi de gun zlar 'gyur te de bzhin ram yis// de ltar nyi ma zla ba'i dbye bas gnyi gar 'gro ba'i dbang las rgyal po yan lag bcu gnyis so// dgun zla 'bring po dang ni tha chungs mngon pa'i mtshams su
31a3(rgyud): chu srin nyi ma song bar ma rig pa// de la rga shi gnyis pa du ni yin te mi'i bdag po skye ba nyi ma gsum par ro// de ltar srid pa la sogs thams cad yan lag bcu gnyis par du rim pas yongs su ba
31a4(rgyud): bar bya'o// de ltar me dang rgya mtsho mda' dang gal te bcu drug 'gyur ba'i dbang las sred par brjod pa'o// phyogs dang chos kyi nyin zhag grangs rnams nyi ma rgyu ba'i dbang las bcu drug cha ni gal te na// dgu
31a5(rgyud): zla tha chungs mtshams su bum par nyi ma song bar gyur na de la 'du byed nyid du brjod// rnam par shes pa de ni gnyis par nyi gnas rab tu yin te ming dang gzugs ni gsum pa ru// de ltar zla ba gnyis su
31a6(rgyud): nalag yin te nyi mo'i dbang las skye dang sdud pa'i sbyor ba las// de yang ma rig la sogs mi mnyam pa'i yan lag gyur pa dge ba'i bya ba rnams la shis// 'du byed la sogs gang zhig mnyam pas
31a7(rgyud): da sa partsod pa gas mams rkyen du rgyas pa'i thugs pa dang chu ba rtso //  khyod po rkyen pa kyis ga na
31a8(rgyud): 'gro'i dbang las yan lag sacu gnyis rnam so// nyi sa dgra drang 'jug rings dal rnams g.yas dang rgyab du sang dag gnas na dgra rnams 'jig par byed// g.yon dang mdun du zhi ba dzi ba'i gar
31b1(rgyud): tshogs mtha' dag rnams ni 'jas pa'i sa ru de bzhin nyid// rnal 'byor ma dang bi Sh+Ti nyid dang ma rgyangs rnams dang rlung ldan pade ster g.yas dang rgyab du'o// g.yon dang mdun du 'chi ba'i gzugs ste mnyam dang / 
31b2(rgyud): mi mnyam gyur pa gnyis ka'i stobs kyis 'chi bar 'gyur// tshangs ma drag mo gzhon nu ma sten nam mkha' 'gro ba'i bdag mo pag me rdo rje lag pa ma'o// tsa mun Ta dang bkra shis ma rnams nor lha'i tshes su
31b3(rgyud): 'gyur ste dang po'i chos kyi dgu pa ru// brgya byin gnod sbyin me'i mtshams dang srin po gshin rje dang ni chu bdag rlung dang dbang ldan du// de ltar 'di ni byed pa de rnams brgyad gnyis dbe ba rnams kyis tshes rnam
31b4(rgyud): 'char ba tha dad do// biSh+Ti rnams ni dkar po'i phyogs la 'char par 'dir 'gyur brgya phyin krashin rje chu lha gnod sbyin du// nag po'i phyogs rnams la yang pas ni me dang srin po rlung dang dbang ldan 'tshams
31b5(rgyud): rnams rim pa yis// drag po shar nas nub phyed 'gro ba nyi ma'i dbang las nyi ma byang du bgrod na bang phyogs su// chu nas me dang ldan par 'gro ba nges pa dang bcas nyi ma lho phyogs bgrod na lho phyogs su// 
31b6(rgyud): shwar nas thun phyed nas naM nab tu zhugs nas rlung dang lho phyogs su yang 'gro ba de basbyin du// dbang ldan chu me gnod sbyin du 'gro srin po rnams la nyi nub bar du bzhu bkang rlung ldan 'di// dpal ldan rtsa ba'i
31b7(rgyud): gcan spangs nas rab tu zhugs ni rlung gi yan lag gnyis 'thab pa las rgya ma// gsum du rtsa ba'i sgra gcan sgra'i stobs rnams 'joms pa de dang mnyam pa gzhon mo yod pa min// mnyam pa dang ni mi
31b8(rgyud): mnyam pa rnams g.yul du 'thab na dbyangs rnams dman pas lhag pas sdig par byed// mi gnyis ngag gi snying la dbugs rnams rab tu zhugs pa gang zhig 'thab mo las ni rgyal bar 'gyur// po nyes pa
32a1(rgyud): por ming brjod pa las rgyal bar 'gyur te phyi nas ming ni brgya par 'gyur ba'o// mtshan ma kha dog dbyangs la sogs pa rnams kyis mnyam dang mi mnyam so 'bras bu med
32a2(rgyud): pa gsungs// 'thab par mi rnams g.yas su dus kye me dang gsom ga che mun pa can du gyur pa na/ ragayul du lha yaM mgon po dang nr-i khyab 'jug pade byed ldan pa mi rnams kyis ni 'joms pa ste/ 
32a3(rgyud): de phyir 'khyog dang drag po lha min 'joms pa dpal ldan rtsa ba'i sgra gcan srid gsum rnam rgyal nyid// shes par bya ba 'thab dus su'i dkyil 'khor sgyur byar yin te gran+dan du dgu rnams 'jig pa min/ 
32a4(rgyud): sa la skar ma dgod pa thub pa dus rnams bya ba dbang po gnod sbyin rgyal pogashin rje ru// 'khor lo de ni 'khor bar 'gyur ba nyin mtshan 'gro ba'i dbang las rig par bya ba mtha' dag go// skar ma gang du
32a5(rgyud): dus me rab yin pa dang mun pa can dag lta ba 'joms par 'gyur pa na// g.yul du 'gra'i sde ni ma lus skad cig gis ltung 'gyur de lto ba'i dbus su rgyal bar 'gyur// sgra gcan dus me dag la gnas

37b7(rgyud): rkang pa lo rnams nyid dang 'khor lo can rnams byung gyur nas// kla k+ki rnams kyi chos 'jig pa dang bde ba dam pa'i rang bzhin rigs gcig pa'i lam ster ba'o// don rnams 'di dag thaMs

38a1(rgyud): rgyas las btus pa// dpal chen po dus kyi 'khor lo zhes bya ba las// 'jig rten khams kyi rnam par dgrong pa ste// // le'u dang po'o// rdzogs smra
38a2(rgyud): / rgyal ba skyed byed khyed kyis rab tu bstan pa'i sna tshogs tshad rnams gang lags bdag gis mi shes pas// slar yang bdag nyid nyan par 'tshal te srid pa gsum po mtha' dag lus rgya
38a3(rgyud): dbus su ji ltar zla ba bzang po'i tshig 'di shin du bde bar gshegs pas gnas nas legs so zhes gsungs gnang ba mdzad// sems can rnams kyi thur pa'i rgyu ru dam pa'i snying rjes lus la yang
38a4(rgyud): sna tshogs chad rnams so// sa chu mo rlung rnams dang rdo rje dang ni lha'i gzhu dang rlung dang khyim gyi 'khor lo dang // zla nyi dag dang sgra gcan lhun po gdeng ka mi dang lha'i gnas dang 'khyog po skar mar bcas/ 
38a5(rgyud): 'pho ba dang ni zla ba phyed bcas dang ni nyin mtshan tshes rnams sa lus lus kyi dbus nyid du// rnal 'byor pa yis shes bya rang rang rigs kyi khyab bdag rnam gsum gnas pa stong pa'i dbye ba yis/ 
38a6(rgyud): lus 'di nyid la ro drag ma lus zos shing mthungs pa lus ni khams rnams tshegs su gyur pa'o// 'byung ba rnams las ro drug nges par rab gsal 'gyur te 'byung ba'i tshogs rnams nam mkha'i
38a7(rgyud): las 'byung / stong pa dang ni ye shes rnam par 'dres par gyur pas ro mnyam pa la 'gyur med rtag pa'o// de ltar 'byung ba la gnas zhi ba srid gsum la gnas gyur pa rang gi lus la rig par bya/ 
38a8(rgyud): pad mar 'jom pa'i sa bon sa yis 'dzin te de las gang zhig phyi nas chu yis skyed par byed// re nyid ro zos pa rnams ma yis smin par byed cing rlung gis 'di nyid 'phel bar byed pa'o// 'phel ba
38b1(rgyud): las ni nam mkhas go skabs 'byed de ma'i bdag po dus kyi dbang gis de ltar grub// rab bskyed dus ni lha mo rnams kyi gnas skabs rnams su byed pa byis pa la sogs dus la'o// sa bon la ni sa
38b2(rgyud): gsol bar lci dang mkhregs par byed ste de ltar chu yis gsher ba nyid// 'di ni me yis smin par byed ste rlung mchog rnam pa bcu po rnams kyis 'phel bar byed pa ste// 'phel ba las ni phyi nas nam mkhas
38b3(rgyud): go skabs 'byed ste dus kyi dbang gis de ltar skye ba'o// gong bu sgra dang yid bcas nus pa rnams ni dngos po sna tshogs du ma rnams kyis spro bar byed// gsang ba'i chu skyes khrag gi dbus su gang tshe byang chub sa bon
38b4(rgyud): srog bcas ltung ba'i tshe// nya dang dus sbal dang ni phag par 'gyur zhing mi yi seng ge mi thung rang sa byed ram dang // nag po sangs rgyas 'dus pa nyid rnams mi dbang bcu ru 'gyur te 'di bcu rnams kyi gnas
38b5(rgyud): skabs kyang rta mngal du rnam pa gsum dang btsa' dus de bzhin gcig ste byis pa yi ni dus kyang gnyis nyid las// gzhon nu lang tshe dag yin rgyas pa gzhan zhes pa ni de bzhin yang dag re re nyid du 'gyur// 
38b6(rgyud): rgyas pa nyid nas zhi ba'i bar la gcig ste srid 'jig mtha' ma rnams ni mngal skyes rnams kyi'o// nyin zhag cung zad par la nya'i gnas skabs nya dang ru sngal nyid kyang ru sbrul rnam par snang // phag pa de nyid
38b7(rgyud): nyi ma'i skye mched rnams ni skye 'gyur gzhan yang mi'i seng ge nyid kyang ngo // mi'u thung la byis pa nyid dang rang byed nas la ma yi bdag po gnyis rgyas skye 'gyur ba dang // slar yang ras so ltung gyur pa de
38b8(rgyud): nag po'i gnas skabs nyid na gsal bar rgyu byed 'gyur// sangs rgyas nyid la zhing dang brtul zhugs dag kyang nges par byed ste rigs gcig la ni 'chi bar 'gyur// khu ba las ni rkang mar rus pa rtsa
39a1(rgyud): 'gyur te khrag las nges par pags pa khrag dang sha/ mda' dbus rtsu ba gcig tu khrag dang sa bon dag las rab tu bskyed pas 'chi med ror gyur pa// phyis nas sa bon myug
39a2(rgyud): las ni rang gi snying khar rtsa ni shin tu 'phra ba rnam pa bcu// lte bar brgyad pa brgyad ste gzhan yang lag pa rkang pa gdong rnams phyi ru 'phel bar 'gyur ba ni// zla ba gnyis pa rdzogs nas lag pa
39a3(rgyud): rka pa gdong rnams cung zud 'dir ni mdo ru bstan pa'o// zla gsum rdzogs nas lag pa rkang pa dag dang mgrin pa rnams kyi rtse mo ma lus mnyam par 'gyur// zla ba bzhin lag pa rkang pa gdong
39a4(rgyud): dang mgrin pa rnams kyi phyogs su rtsa ni phra mo rnams// zla ba lnga par sha rnams la ni rten pa'i rus pa nam mkha' ro dang me dang tshig rnams kyang ngo // zla ba drug pa la yang sha dang khrag dang tshor ba bde
39a5(rgyud): dang ni sdug bsngal rnams su 'gyur// thub pa mchog la smin ma dang ni skra dang bug pa smra rnams kyang ste zla ba'i rjes nyid la// nyin zhag so so'i dus su rtsa rnams rab tu 'phel ba stongs sde mig gi grangs
39a6(rgyud): as kyis// gnad dang rus pa rnams dang rkang dang ror ldan dri chen dri chu rnams ni brgyad pa nyid la'o// 'ug pa zhes par skye ba'i dus su de la skye gnas kyis bsdams mi zad sdug bsngal chen por
39a7(rgyud): 'gyur// mngal du mngal gnas nyid dang skye ba'i dus dang byis pa'i rang bzhin rnams kyis mi bzang sdug bsngal le// gzhon nu lang tsho dag la bud med nor dang bkra shis 'dod pas nyon mongs sdug
39a8(rgyud): bsngal chen pos gang // rgas dang 'chi ba'i skye ba'i sdug bsngal chen po dag ste slar yang du 'phod la sogs 'gro drug 'jigs ster ba// 'gro ba 'di rnams ma lus sgyu ma la rmongs gyur pas sdug
39b1(rgyud): bsngal ba las sdug bsngal gyur pa'o// 'khor ba'i nang nas gal te mi nyid dag tu gyur kyang chos kyi blo ni brgya lam zhig na'o// de las dge ba'i dbang gis sangs rgyas nyid la rjes chags 'gyur da
39b2(rgyud): dang po'i theg par rab tu 'jug/ de las dpal ldan rdo rje'i theg pa dang ni ma lus snying po bsgom pa'i blo 'jug brgya lam na'o// de las sangs rgyas nyid ste 'dod mchog bde ba'i go 'phang mo 'jug
39b3(rgyud): e ma shin tu dka' ba'o// mngal du yang dag dag pa'i sku ste skye ba'i dus nas so skye'i bar nyid chos kyi sku// so rnams rjes pa'i bar gyis rgyal ba'i long spyod rdzogs skor nges par 'gyur ro mi
39b4(rgyud): bdag skye/ de nas nges par mi rnams 'chi ba'i mtha' ru sprul pa'i sku ru rab tu gsol bar brjod pa ste// slar yang 'dir ni ye shes rnams shes dbye bas mngal dang phyi ru rnam pa bzhi ru 'gyur
39b5(rgyud): pa'o// slar yang rnam shes zla ba nyi ma pad mar 'dres par gyur pa rnams ni mngal du dag pa'i sku// khams dang phung po rnam pa bcu po skye bar 'gyur ba gang zhig rgyal ba'i chos skur 'gyur ba'o// 
39b6(rgyud): de nas rna ba sgra la sogs pa skye ba yon tan dbang las long spyod rdzogs pa'i ska ru 'gyur// de nas rna ba sgra la sogs pa skye ste mngal nas skye ba'i dus 'di sma yI ska ru brjod pa'o// gang zhig skyes nas
39b7(rgyud): dbugs dpung ba ni nges par de nyid dag pa'i sku ru rab tu 'gyur bar nges// de nas gang zhig sa skye gyur nas tshig mi gsal bar slar yang de bzhin chos kyi sku ru brjod// de nas gnyis skye ba rjes
39b8(rgyud): rjes pa rgyal ba'i long spyod rdzogs par 'gyur ro mi yi bdag po kye// so rnams rjes nas 'chi ba'i mthar thug rgyal ba'i bdag po'i sprul pa'i sku ru 'gyur de phyi rol tu// ye shes dang ni rnam
40a1(rgyud): shes 'dres pa'i nyi ma ri beng can bcas yo shos rdo rje la sogs rnams// mngal du sku rdo rje la sogs rnams// mngal du sku rdo rje la sogs pa stobs dang ldan pa yang dag rim pas
40a2(rgyud): 'byung bar 'gyur ba ni// drang por mngal 'dir dpal ldan skra yi rdo rjer 'gyur ste gsung gi rang bzhin rab tu skyes pa'i dus// se rnams skyes pa nges par thugs ste slar yang byung nas skyes pa ye shes
40a3(rgyud): rdo rjer gyur pa'o// sa yi snying por me nyid du ni 'gyur ste stong pa'i snying por sa dang rlung dag nyid kyang ngo // rlung dang sa nyid dag gi snying por chu nyid 'gyur ste rang bzhin med dang rang bzhin bcas pa yin// 
40a4(rgyud): sa yi rten ni chu ste slar yang chu'i mer brjod me'i 'dir ni rten nyid rlung zhes bya ba'o// rlung gi stong pa yin te ji ltar rten dang rten pa rnams kyi tshul du rab tu 'gyur ro mi bdag kye// phung po'i rten ni 'byung ba
40a5(rgyud): rnams su 'gyur te mchog gi lus la 'byung ba'i tshogs kyi rtsa rnams so// rtsa rnams kyi ni srog gi rlung 'gyur rnam pa bcu ru 'gyur ste srog gi rlung gi sems dpa'o// sems kyi rang bzhin gnyis su
40a6(rgyud): 'gyur te yon tan dbang las rang bzhin bcas dang rang bzhin med pa yi// rten du 'gyur ba'i gtso bo de ni srid po gsum pas phyag byas kun 'gro gzhom du med pa'o// sa las dri skyed pa ste yang ni
40a7(rgyud): me las ro dang chu las gzugs kyi khams kyi rnam pa'o// rlung las reg bya nyid dang zhi ba las kyang sgra ste nam mkha' las ni chos kyi dbyings nyid do// stong pas sgra rnams 'dzin par byed ste nges par rgyal
40a8(rgyud): skyed byed pas chos kyi dbyings dang rlung nyid kyis// dri dang chu yis me'i rang bzhin ro dang gzugs ste sa yis rlung ste reg bya nyid kyang ngo // srid pa gsum gyi gnas su sa las gzugs su grub
40b1(rgyud): sto yang ni chu las 'du shes grub par 'grub par 'gyur// me las nges par tshor ba rab tu brjod ste rlung las 'du byed phung por 'gyur bar nges pa'o// nam mkha' rdo rje dag las rnam par shes dang ye shes 'gyu
40b2(rgyud): ste 'dir ni drug pa 'dres pa'i lus// khams dang phung po la sogs thams cad khrag dang byang chub sems la sogs pa sbyor ba la ni 'gyur// rna ba rdo rje'i rang bzhin yin ste sems ni nam mkha'i rang
40b3(rgyud): bzhin 'gyur ro mi'i bdag po kye// sna ni sa yi rang bzhin 'gyur te de ltar ro ma zhes su brjod pa'i me'i rang bzhin 'gyur ba'o// mig ni chu yi rang bzhin nyid dang srid pa gsum gyi gnas su rlung gi rang bzhin
40b4(rgyud): lus pa'o// de ltar rna ba la sogs thams cad yon tan dbang las 'gyur te ye shes rnam shes sbyor ba las// lus kyi mchog la ye shes khams su ser snar 'gyur te nam mkha' khams las zhes
40b5(rgyud): sdang rdo rje'i/ rlung las phrag dog rdo rjer rab tu gsal bar gsungs ste de bzhin me las 'dod chags rdo rje'o// chu las nga rgyal sa las gti mug dag tu 'gyur ste rang bzhin dbang las yon tan rnams
40b6(rgyud): su 'gyurate/ ngag rkang lag pa gshad pa'i lam rnams rlung dang me dang tu dang sa rnams las ni 'gyur ba'o// ye shes khams su thur sel rnam pa gsum zhes bya bar 'gyur ste stong pa las kyang srog gi
40b7(rgyud): rlung / rlung gi dbus nas mnyam dang me las slar yang gyen du rgyu bar brjod dang chu las khyab byed nyid// sa las rlung dang de nas ru sbal rtsangs pa lha sbyin nor rnams las ni rgyal ba rnams kyi rlung // bzhi
40b8(rgyud): baM rnams ni rlung dang me dang chu dngas rnams nyid las rim pas rab tu 'gyur ba'o// stong pa'i khams las lha dang mi rnams kyi ni gtsug gtor 'gyur te ye shes khams las gsang ba'o// gsal
41a1(rgyud): rlung gi khams las snying kar pad mar 'gyur te nges par me las mgrin pa'i 'khor lo smras// chu las sman ma'i dbus kyi pad ma dang ni sa la sa nor dang nor kyang s+ya sde ba'i
41a2(rgyud): pad ma dag/ rkang pa lag pa dag la tshigs drug sa dang chu dang me dang rlung rnams gsum gyi grangs kyis so// sa la sogs pa khams lnga yon tan gsum gyi rang bzhin nyid las rkang pa lag pa dag tu
41a3(rgyud): gyur/ 'theb mo la sogs sor mo bcu la gsum gyis bsgyur ba'i tshigs kyi tshogs rnams mtha' dag gyur pa rnams// de rnams sen mo'i mtha' ru yang dag gzung ste slar yang so rnams de nyid rab tu
41a4(rgyud): dbye ba yis// gang zhig gzhan yang lus mchog pa spu'i mtha' ru yin te de nyid de'i khams su rig par bya// gsang ba gtsug gtor dang ni lte ba rnams ni lhan cig skyes pa rgyal ba'i sku ni rang bzhin
41a5(rgyud): med/ snying ka'i 'khor lor chos kyi sku ru 'gyur te thig le'i pad mar yang ni sprul pa'i sku nyid dang // mgrin par long spyod rdzogs pa'i sku ru yang dag 'gyur te yon tan dbang la rims kyis lhag pa'i lha
41a6(rgyud): snying ka'i 'khor lo mgrin pa'i 'khor lo spyi bre'i pad mar chos dang lcong spyod rdzogs dang dag pa'o// lte ba mgrin pa gsung ba spyi bo snying ka rnams dang de bzhin gtsug gtor dbus nyid rnams la ni/

41b1(rgyud): rang bzhin yon tan dbang las kha dog rnams kyi dbye bas rnal 'byor ldan pas rig par bya ba ste// kha dog ser po nag po dmar po dkar po rnams ni sa dang rlung dang me dang chu rnams la// ye shes nam
41b2(rgyud): mkha' dag kyang lus dang bsam pa'i rab tu dbye bas sngo dang ljang khu dag tu 'gyur// shes rab thabs dag rus pa dang ni sha ste chu dang khrag bcas pa dang me dang lci ba nyid// rlung dang gshang ba dag
41b3(rgyud): rang stong pa khu ba dpal ldan rdul dang byang sems mchog gi lus la 'gyur// gzhan yang rna ba sgra la sogs pa rang gi rgyal ba'i rigs kyi dbang las ngag gi rang bzhin sogs// de ltar lha mo rnaMs
41b4(rgyud): dang sangs rgyas rnams bcas yul dang yul ba can dkyil 'khor la ni brjod par bya// stong phrag drug gi rtsa rnams nyi byed kyis bsgyur ba yis mngal gyi dbus su rab tu byed pa dang // ri bong 'dzin
41b5(rgyud): pa spangs nas la nyid longs pa'i bar rnams la ni rab tu 'phel bar byed pa'o// lo rnams bcu gnyis par la'ang rang lus la nyi mi khams rnams 'phel ba dang ni spong ba ste// nyin dang nyin la zung
41b6(rgyud): gi grangs kyi rim pa'i dbye bas skyes nas rtsa rnams 'chad par 'gyur pa'o// dpal ldan 'byung ba rnams dang dbyang po rnams ni bcu ru 'gyur te las kyi dbang po lnga rnams dang // de tsam lngar gsu
42a1(rgyud): brjod ste tshar pa 'di na bdud dur 'gyur// rdo sgra dang dbang pa gzhu dang dashad pa yangs chu tshong dbugs 'thung 'jug pa'i zung dan go// zung 'di dag ri dbu brgya
42a2(rgyud): 'gyur rnams kyis 'grol gcis kyin thug pa'i dbye bas skan ma rnams/ me rgyu skam so so'i rnam pa nyid ste nyim 'gas su'i chu tshed rnams ni tshigs kyi dbye bar 'gyur// mu rnams chub chu brnam
42a3(rgyud): dang rgyu ma sprin dang ri bong can gzhan cha dag khams rnams rang bzhin gnyis// ba spu shig rnams dang ni srin bu khu ba rnams ni 'byung ba'i skye gnas rnam pa bzhi rnams s+ho// dga' ba la sogs sor mo
42a4(rgyud): tshigs dang mgo bo'i pad ma dang ni lte ba'i pad mar rdzogs pa'o// tshangs granas mtho ris 'jig rten nyid ste mchog gi lag rkang dag gi mi yul sa 'og 'jig rten s+ho// rgya mtsho'i gling dang ri rnams
42a5(rgyud): gsher dang 'jam dang sra ba rnams kyi khams rnams gsum gyi rang bzhin no// pa tsha'i rgya mtsho me dag 'dir ni gcig ste bskyod pa'i dkyil 'khor khrag dang pags pa rgyal po kye// spu rnams mtha' dag
42a6(rgyud): rab tu rdzogs pa snyid gsum gnas su du sa'i dbye ba rnams kyis 'grub pa'o// bsnying dang mgrin pa'i lte ba'i pad ma rdo rje nyi ma me rnams rim pas yang dag sprob pa// gzhu'i rnam pa rnam pa nyid
42a7(rgyud): nyi ma som so sbyin sreg rgya mtsho'i zur ldan tha khud du// de rnams kyi ni steng du me mchog dri med 'od zer 'phro ba ye shes sku ste mun pa'i mthar// gang du nyi ma klog gis sreg min ri bong 'dzin rna
42a8(rgyud): skar ma la sogs snang ba med// gza' rnams snying kA'i pad ma'i 'dab ma rnarmas ste gsol bar chu tshod lto ba'i phad ma drug bcu'o// smin ma'i dbus su zla ba'i rkang po ma na yin to long sbed 'khor
42b1(rgyud): le rgyu skar mi bdag kye// pad ma'i lte bar rgyu skar rnams kyi slar yang chu tshod rnams su rnal 'byor rnams kyi rig bya ba/ chu tshod rnams la chu srang rnams ste gsal bar mtha' dag lus kyi lag rkang
42b2(rgyud): la sogs chags kyang ngo // lte ba'i chu skyes nyi ma 'dab mar mchog gi cha rnams 'khor ba rim pas 'pho bar 'gyur ba ni// sreg zung rnams kyi 'pho ba dgu brgya nyis 'gyur rnams kyis kar ka Ta'i dus
42b3(rgyud): sbyor mi dbang kye// dus sbyor gang la nyi ma gnas pa nyin mtshan 'khor ba de nyid de ru rig par bya ba ni// dus sbyor tshad rnams shes par bya ste bu lon nor du g.yas dang g.yon du mnyam par bgrod pa'o// 
42b4(rgyud): pad ma'i 'dab ma re rer nub kyi phyogs su sa dang byang du chu dag rab tu rgyu ba'o// lho ru me dang shar du rab tu rgyu ba rlung ste gzhan yang 'dab ma'i dbus su stong pa'o// 'pho ba lnga'i dbye ba rnams kyi mtshams
42b5(rgyud): nas rab tu rgyu ba drug bcu'i dbus las dman pa'o// de ltar 'pho ba'i bye ba rnams ni nyin zhag so so'i dus su dus sbyor rnams kyis dbye bar 'gyur// stong pa la sogs de nyid lnga rnams byung nas nges
42b6(rgyud): par rab tu rgyu ste sa la sogs pa g.yas// sgra gcan dus me dag dang zla ba nyi ma gza' lhag skyes sa pa ba sangs dang bla ma dang // 'jug rings ngal ba rnams ni nam mkha' la sogs dkyil 'khor rnams
42b7(rgyud): la bdag po bcu rnams zhing can 'gyur// g.yon du zla ba dbang por 'gyur te g.yas phyogs su ni nyi ma nyid do mi bdag kye// de yi steng du snying ka'i phyogs na nor gyi 'dab ma'i rtswa'i 'khor lo rnams ni yang
42b8(rgyud): dag gnas pa'o// sreg la sogs pa rlung gi tshogs rnams ri be'i ba can dang nyi ma me rnams g.yon dang g.yas dang dbus// g.yen gyi zla ba'i rtsa nas ri bong can mtshon yin te g.yas kyi nyi ma las ni
43a1(rgyud): khrag nyid do// drabs nas dus me'i rang bzhin dus stong rnams kyi 'tshams su drug bcu'i dbugs las dman pa rgyu ba'o// nor gyi pad ma'i 'dab mar srog dang thur du rgyu dang
43a2(rgyud): mnyam gnas rkyen du rgyu ba'i rlung rnams dang // khyab byed dang ni kA dang nu sbal dag dang rtsongs pa gzhan yang lha min nor rgyal rlung rnams te// de ltar rtsa'i 'khor lor las kyi dbye bas rlung rnams rnam
43a3(rgyud): phapa bcu ru yang dag gnas pa ni// star ma la sogs rdu can mthar thug d+ha 'i 'khor le mtha' dag rnams ni snying ka'i pad ma'o// srog gis srog ldan byed cing nyi ma ri bong can nyid lam nas 'gro/ 
43a4(rgyud): ste bza' btung mtha' dag rnams// 'og tu khyer ba mthur du rgyu ba yin ste lus la ma lus ro mnyam byed pa mnyam par brjod// lus la skyong byed gyen du rgyu bar brjod par kha dang lag pa rkang pas
43a5(rgyud): glu gar byed pas so// na de nyid byed pas khyab byed zhes ma cang bzhin yon tan dbang las de bzhin lus 'joms byed pas so// kla yis bsgregs pa nyid ste gsal bar lag pa dang ni rkang pa 'gums
43a6(rgyud): par byed pa ru sprul lo// khro dang 'khrug pa mtha' dag rtsangs pa'i rlung gis byed ste dbul bar byed pa lha sbyin nyid kyis so// lus la lnga 'gyur mtha' yang rlung cig gis ni myi gtong pa de nor rgyal
43a7(rgyud): nyid ste mi bdag kye// de ltar srog waM sregs pa'i rlung rnams thams cad kyis ni rang bzhin gyur pa'i yon tanar+NaMs mi 'dir// ser skya phrag mo lug ste rtsa rnams lam gsum nyid du gnas pa stso
43a8(rgyud): dang ni glang chen lde// rgyal nyid drug pang ni rgyal ba 'gro med 'phyang ba nor ste dpal ldan kun ku he dgu pa'o// dung can phyogs kyi grangs te gang zhig byang chub sa bon bde ba'i mthar ni 'jog go
43b1(rgyud): bdag kyi/ de ltar dpal sprin rtsa ba'i 'khor lo tshigs kyi dbye ba du mas rnam pa mang por 'gyur ba'o// dbang po me dang gshin brje bden bral chu ltar bcas pa rlung dang nor dang dbang ldan nyid rnams kyis
43b2(rgyud): gnas 'di rnams su gnas pa nyid mo mtshan mo la ni de'i rang bzhin rgyu zhing long spyod do// de stengs mgrin pa'i 'khor lor gza' tshogs dang bcas rgyu skar 'khor lo yang dag gnas par brjod pa'o// 
43b3(rgyud): tshangs pa'i gnas gyur dpal ldan dpral bar dpangs kyis yongs bskor ba la thig le dkar po nges par mdzag/ rtsa bar sa dang g.yon du chu nyid rab tu yin te g.yas su byin za dang ni steng du rlung
43b4(rgyud): dbus su nam mkha' yin te sna'i bug pa gnyis pa dag nas rim pas mnyam par rab tu rgyu// 'di rnams nus pas rab tu phug nas mchog gi rang bzhin 'gro zhing bcu gnyis mtha' nas cha mtha'
43b5(rgyud): sa pa/ zhing la sogs pa lag pa rkang pa dag gi pad ma gnyis kyi sor mo ma lus rnams kyi mthar// 'khor lo can ni rang gi lus la rdo rje can ste lnga mchog bdag po yan lag bcu gnyis 'gog/ 
43b6(rgyud): rigs gcig yang dag ye shes yin te shing rta mngal gzhug pa rnams 'phags pa'i tshad med do// drag po rang rgyal ming can nyid du rab 'gyur ste ha nu man ta nyan thos srog chags so// ma rungs
43b7(rgyud): kA klo'i dbang po sdig pa nyid ste gcod byed sdug bsngal ster nyid mi dge ba'i lam// rta yi stobs nyid ma rig pa ste lha min stobs ni bdud kyi phyogs rnams bzhi po ma lus pa'o// de rnams 'thab
43b8(rgyud): bsdud pa srid pa'i 'jigs 'joms pa ste rmel bas dpal dang ldan pa thar pa'i lam// ka la sha ru chos ster srid pa'i 'joms pa po ste rdzas kyis gang ba'i sa nyid khams dag pa// bu ga
44a1(rgyud): / dang ci'i bla ma bram ze lha dbang rgya dang mdun du 'byung bar 'gyur ba'o// srang gsum rnam par rgyal ba 'jas dpal 'jig rten mgon dag dpal ldan rdul 'ang byang chub
44a2(rgyud): bon no// sa stengs rgyab du bram ze la sogs sna tshogs rigs ni rnam par dag pa'i sangs rgyas du ma'o// de ltar kla klo'i dbang po nges par 'thab par 'gyur pa lus can rnams kyi lus kyi dbus su'o// 
44a3(rgyud): phyiraru rgyu ma'i ngo bo nyid kyi nges yin nam mkha'i yul du kla klo'i 'thab me 'thab pa min// dus lo me'i grangs ste lo nyid nyin khrag tshogs kyis bsgyur ba 'grod pa'i dbye bas rigs drug 'gyur
44a4(rgyud): sum bcu'i chus thob zla ba sum bcu rtsa drug ro la ro yis bsgyur ba rnal 'byor mi rnams rigs// gza'i dbye bas cha thob pa rnams nges par rab tu gsol bar dus kyi 'khor lo'i lha rnams so// 
44a5(rgyud): phyed kyi dbye bas lha dang lha mo rnams su mngon par brjod 'gyur mi bdag kye// nyin zhag yan lag las ni sgyu 'phrul dra ba rnam pa gsum du 'gyur te bug pa rig byed dang // slar yang 'byung ba rgya mtsho
44a6(rgyud): dang ni me dang tu gter dag tu 'gyur ste dpal ldan dus dbye bas// de nyid zhes bya ba dang gzhan yang drug gis dman dang slar yang de dag phyed kyi dbye bas ste// phyis ni gnyis kyi dbye ba bsres
44a7(rgyud): bcu gsum dgu phyogs rnams/ dang drug pa de nyid dang bcas rnams// zla ba'i tshe'i nyin zhag tshogs khas nges par gza'i cha yis thob par 'gyur ba nyin zhag drug po nyid// rdo rje can gyi
44a8(rgyud): gzhan yang nyin zhag tshogs lhag sku gsung thugs kyi phyag rgya'o// shes rab thabs dag sku la gsum gnas rnal 'byor ma dang rnal 'byor rgyud du nges par rab tu gsal/ 
44b1(rgyud): nu mas khro bo dag rnams rim pas bcu cu rab tu 'gyur ste sangs rgyas lha mo rnams ni lnga// gzugs la sogs pa rnams dang dmigs sogs drug ste slar yang lha'i tshogs rnams drug gnyis mi'i bdag po kye/ 
44b2(rgyud): rnal 'byor ma dang klu dang gtum po brgyud du gnas pa 'di rnams thams cad nyis 'gyur brjod pa'o// 'di rnams dpal ldan dus kyi 'khor lo bzhi yis lhag pa'i brgya dang de'i byed ni gnas gsum la'o// 
44b3(rgyud): nyi ma'i rgya la zla ba'i nyin zhag so so'i nang nas chu tshod drug bcu rnams ni nges 'byung // rnal 'byor ma rnams dus sbyor dang bsres de rnams mtha' dag gnyis kyis bsgyur ba srid gsum gnas su'o// nyi
44b4(rgyud): ma'i cha la nyin zhag rab tu phye ba gnyis kyis bskur ba'i rnal 'byor ma'i tshogs rnams 'dir// marjod pa dang bcas mtha' dag bsdus par gyur pa rnams ni nyi ma'i yon tan gsum gyi nyin zhag rnams
44b5(rgyud): nyin byed la nI lo'i dbye bar 'gyur zhing ri bong 'dzin la phyogs kyi dbye bar mtha' dag go// de ltar dang po'i sangs rgyas la ni mkha' lhag mi'i bdag po rnams kyi lha dang lha mo rnams// thabs dang shes
44b6(rgyud): rab nyin mo mtshan mor 'gyur te mam nya mtsha snyed dang ni nyin mo phyed nyid do// nyin mtshan dus kyi yang dag zla ba'i 'pho ba'i dbye bas gang gis rang gi lus la shes pa'i// de ni dpal ldan 'jam pa'i rdo rjes srid
44b7(rgyud): 'jigs bcom nas skye ba 'di nyid la ni sangs rgyas 'gyur// sum bcu cha yis 'thob dang de las gsum gyis bsgyur ba'i lha dang bdag po dus kyi 'khor lo dang // phyi rol du ni phyag rgya drug ste/ 
44b8(rgyud): gzhan yang de nas de bzhin du ni rtsa ba'i 'khor lo dang // spyi gtsug du ni rgya mtsho snying kar brgyad dang mgo bar mi'i bdag po mgrin par so'i grangs rnams dang // lte bar brgyad kyis brgyad bsgrar
45a1(rgyud): rnams dang mi'i bdag po nyis 'gyur gsang ba'i dbus su rab tu 'grub// rtsa drug 'khor lo 'gog 'gyur bcu yis yul rnams 'joms ste de rnams 'dus pa'i rang bzhin rnams su
45a2(rgyud): brjod// yang dang yang du nyis 'gyur du yang bsgyur bas bad ga na dang ni 'khris pa rlung gi cha rnams so// de rnams kyis ni nges par 'chi ba ster zhing bla ma'i nges pa'i dbang las tshe dang nad med ste// 'khor
45a3(rgyud): drug la dus kyi rtsa yis 'chi ba'i 'jigs 'joms rnal 'byor rnams la 'dir ni ngo mtshar med// spyi gtsug tu ni rgya mtsho dpral bar chu gter dus kyis bsgyur bas bad kan khaMs rnaMs rab 'khrugs byed// 
45a4(rgyud): mgrin par so dang snying kha'i chu skyes la ni dmig gis dus bsgyur mkhris pa'i khams rnams rab 'khrug byed// lte bar rgya mtsho drug bcu skar yang gi sang bar mi bdag de bzhin rlung gi khams ni rang
45a5(rgyud): 'khrug byed// gzhan yang gsang bar phyogs dang drug po gsungs pa rnams kyis nges par 'dus par 'gyur zhing 'gog pa'o// rtsa drug 'khor lo dgag gsungs lam nyid rnam gsum 'gro ba zla ba/ 
45a6(rgyud): nyi ma me'i dbye bas so// de dag lus la bsrung bar 'gyur ba bla ma'i nges pa'i dbang gis sreg chags gang la 'chi ster ba// drug rnams gang tshe srog 'jug 'gyur na mi rnams nyid la rgyun du 'chi ba spe// 
45a7(rgyud): bar nges// phra mo ru ni srog mi 'jug na rnal 'byor pa rnams 'chi ba'i yul nyid gang gis gcod par byed// gang zhig srog ni nyin dang mtshan du rtsa nyid cig nas rgyun dus lo'i bar du 'tshe bar 'gyur/ 
45a8(rgyud): rgyun mi 'chad pa par rgyun mi rnams kyi ni phyed bcas lo'i tshe ru 'gyur// zla ba gcig tu rnam par mi 'chad rgyun 'tshe ba zla ba gsum gnas mi'i bdag po kye// de ltar rnal 'byor rang
45b1(rgyud): gi lus la ri bong can song 'chi ba dus kyi 'khor los shes par byed// nyin zhig lnga nas nyi shu rtsa lngar gyur gyi bar du lnga lnga 'grod cing 'phel bar byed pa dang // de nas re res bgred pa rdzogs pa'i dus da
45b2(rgyud): bcu la gsum gyis bsgyur dang gsum nyid lhag pa'i// de srid par la mnyam ste de rnams gsum mag ri bong can dang drug dang gsum zung zla ba rnams// zla ba de rnams lhag mnyin zhag tshes phyogs
45b3(rgyud): mda' dang yon tan gnyis dang zla ba'i 'tshe ba'o// rang gnas khyim gyi 'khor lo cha mchog nyid kyis 'dor ste 'chi ltas lhag ma rnams ni mtshungs pa las// lo dang zla ba dang ni nyin zhag rnams kyis gsum mig ri
45b4(rgyud): bong can dang drag gsum zung zla ste// nyi ma mnyam par rdzogs na nges par 'chi ltas nyid de tshes phyogs mda' dang yon tan lte bar zhugs// nyin zhag sum bcu rtsa drug rnams kyi mtha' ru nyin phyed 'chi ltas sgro/ 
45b5(rgyud): ba yis ni 'chi bar 'gyur// shar du lo gsum nyin zhag tshogs las mda' dang 'jig rten rnams kyis dor bar byed pa'o// de nas bgrod bcas mda' dus me ru nges ste mkha' ri zla ba rnams ni gsum pa nyid la'o// 
45b6(rgyud): mig dang kA dang ri dang mda' dang de bzhin gzhan yang nor dang lag pa bdun pa dag la gnas// de na rtswa la sogs pa nyin zhag tshogs rnams thams cad de ltar lte ba yi ni rabar nyid do// dus kyi lo nas nyin zhag
45b7(rgyud): 'gro ba'i dbang las ji srid rgyu ba yang dga'apho ba'i bar du'o// zla ba zhes pa dang ni nyi ma'i lam nas mnyam dang mi mnyam nyin zhog cig gi rim pas 'phel// gzhan yang 'pho ba'i dbang gis mi mnyam mnyam
45b8(rgyud): zhag rnams kyis bcu gnyis rtsibs la spong bar byed// ji srid phyed dang bcas pa'i zla ba'i bar dang bcu la gsum gyis bsgyur dang 'tsho ba'i nyin mtshan gsum// dbugs dang chu srang chu tshod rnams dang nyin
46a1(rgyud): zhag nyid dang dus rnams la ni rim pas 'phel bas ste// lo bdun bgrod pa'i yan log dang ni drag bcu'i lo rnams la yang bgrod par 'gre ba'i dbang gis so// sum bcu'i
46a2(rgyud): rnams zla ba gsum gyis dbye ste nyin zhag 'gro ba'i dbang las dus lo zla ba phyed// dus 'khor lus ni gsum bcu gnyis phyed dang bcas pa'i bgos pa'i nyin zhag tshogs rnams 'phel bar
46a3(rgyud): 'gyur/ lte ba'i 'khor lo log pas 'gro la dgus bsgyur phyogs dang phyogs kyis rtsa rnams 'chad par 'gyur ba'o// tshigs rnams re re'i rtsa la nyin zhag rnams kyis spong ba las kyi 'khor lo dang ni bya ba
46a4(rgyud): stan/ mgrin par rgyu skar rtsa rnams zla ba'i dbus su rim pas nyin dang nyin las spong bar 'gyur ba'o// thig le la gnas zla phyed dbus su ri bong can rkang snying kar gza' rtsa gsang gnas rnams la spong // 
46a5(rgyud): sde tshan rnams ni dbyangs dang bcas rnams nyin phyed 'pho ba bgrod pa'i khyim gyi dbye ba rnams kyis ste// pi nas de res lhag pas 'phel dang rim min nyin dang nyin zhag dus kyi lo nyid bar du'o// lo gcig
46a6(rgyud): nas ni zla phyed gsum gyi dbus su dbyangs dang nyin zhag dbang las 'phel nas 'chi ba dang // 'tsho ba'i nyin dang mtshan mo gcig gis dus kyis dbugs 'byin pa dang dbugs rngub pa rnams mdzad par
46a7(rgyud): 'gyur// lte ba mgrin pa dpral ba snying kha'i pad ma rnams dang rtsa gzhan lhag ma dang bcas pa rnam la// gnas pa nyi ma ro dang rang snying pad mar thun phyed dang bcas chu tshod de bzhin du// rkang pa lag
46a8(rgyud): pa'i tshigs rnams la ni tshes la dus kyi 'khor lo bsgyur dang nyin zhag drag pa'i bar nyid ste// mtha' ru phra mo thams cad rab tu rgyu ba nyin zhag gcig gis snying ka'i chu skyes spong bar 'gyur// lo ba
46b1(rgyud): nyin zhag tshogs ste stong phrag gsum bcu rtsa drug rnams la zung gi rtsa yis 'phel ba'o// gang dang gang gi nyin mtshan dus la nyi ma zla ba rang rang rdzogs pa'i long spyod nus pa med// nyi ma'i nyin zhag nyi
46b2(rgyud): ma'i long spyod la ni bu len du 'gyur zla ba'i long spyod de'i phyed// rgyu skar nyin zhag dbye bas nyi ma ri bong can dag rgyu ba zla bas stongs ste spangs pa rnams// lus la srog lhag pa ni gsal bar 'pho ba'i
46b3(rgyud): bar du rkang spangs rig byed kyis dman drug bcu ste// 'pho ba ma lus dbye ba rnams kyis nyin zhag so so'i dus la rtsa zung nges par 'joms pa'o// lo nyid gzhan dang gzhan gyi dbus su nyi ma ri bong can
46b4(rgyud): rgyu ba las stong mig ri'i grangs// lha mi rnams kyi rang rang tshe'i tshad kyis de ltar lo brgya rnams kyis dus kyis 'pho bar byed// mi rnams dus rgyu'i tshe na sos btab pa 'am nad dam chung zad rma ru gyur
46b5(rgyud): pra na/ de la brten nas myur bar rtsa ba'i 'khor lo rnams su dus nyid thegs pa med par 'jug/ 'khor lo rnams kyi rtsa nyid 'gags te nyi ma ri bong can 'gro mtha' dag gcod par byas nas kyang // 
46b6(rgyud): gang zhig la ni dbus su phra mo la rten srog chags rnams kyi srog nyid 'phro go mi bdag kyang // snying ka'i pad ma dang ni dpal ldan dpral bar long spyod lte ba'i 'khor lo rnams la zla ba'i// rkang pa
46b7(rgyud): rgyub 'byung phyogs chos dang bcu la dgu ldan pa dang drag po zung dang rgyal ba dang // de nyid rnams ni nyin zhag bdun phrag rnams kyis spong ste slang yong rim pas ri bong can// thig le gang bar rab
46b8(rgyud): tu byas ste yang ni snying kar dkar po'i phyogs la nor du 'jug/ slar yang nag por de bzhin bu lon 'jug pa rkang pa dang ni rkang pa lte ba'i pad ma'i bar// snying ka mgo bos rtsibs brgyad pa dang / 
47a1(rgyud): / bcu drug rtsibs ni de bzhin du skyes gnag dang dkar ba nyid// mgrin par sum bcu rtsa gnyis rtsibs dang gzhan yang lte bar nyis 'gyur dmar po dang ni ser po'o// brgyud pa gnyis
47a2(rgyud): ni mgrin pa lte ba las ste mgo dang snying kar dkar dang gnag po gang ba'o// a sogs ha ya ra wa lar ldan dbyangs rnams sum bcu thig le dpal ldan tsheg drag gis phye na// drug bcur 'gyur ste
47a3(rgyud): de rnams dus dang mi bdag kA dang se'i ge sar rtse mo rnams la'o// ka sogs sde tshan rnams la thig le a dang A dang bi sar rga yis phye na pad mchog 'dab// nyi sha lhag pa'i tshigs brgya rnams
47a4(rgyud): la thun gyi 'gro ba'i dbang gis nyi ma 'phel dang 'grib pa'o// zla phyed du zla ba nyid rgyu ba la nyin zhag cig gi rkang pas bu lon du yang byed// slar yang zla ba gnyis la nyin zhag nyid kyis 'brel bar 'gyur
47a5(rgyud): te gzhan yang lo nyid stor ba yis// gang ba'i lo la nyin zhag drug tu 'gyur te yang ni de bzhin 'chi ba'i mtshams su 'phel ba'o// de bzhin 'dir ni nyi mar gnyis 'gyur dag tu lo dang lo la bu lon 'phe
47a6(rgyud): lo mi bdag kye// dbugs drug gis ni chu srang gcig tu rab tu 'gyur te chu srang drug bcus chu tshod zhes su brjed// chu tshod drug bcus nyin zhag nyid du 'gyur te nyin zhag sum bcu 'gyur ba rnams kyis zla ba
47a7(rgyud): gcig/ zla ba drug gis bgod par 'gyur ste bgrod pa nyis gyur dag gis lo gcig tu ni rab tu grub// skyes bu rnams kyis cher 'gyur lo brgya rnams la bu lon 'gro ba dus kyi rtsa yi dbang gis so// 
47a8(rgyud): 'jig rten gsum na lha dang lha min mi rnams nang nas rang gi lus la nyi zla rgyu ba dag/ rnal 'byor stobs kyis gang pa nus pa med pa zla bas nyin zhag tshogs la longs mi spyod pa dang // nyi mas rgyu
47b1(rgyud): skar thams cad la ni srid par lo nyid dbus su rim pas long spyod pas so// lo dang le'i nang nas bu lon gyis 'bring dus kyi 'khor lo gcig nyid dpa' bas srid pa 'joms// gang gis rtsa gcig chad par gyur
47b2(rgyud): na gcin ni skyur mo nyid du 'gyur ro mi bdag kye// gong bu rnam par 'chad pa'i dus su de tsam lnga ni nyin zhag lnga dang mchog gi cha spong ba// rna bar sgra dang kha yis nges par ro rnams spong ba yin te mig gi
47b3(rgyud): dbus su gzugs nyid do// sna yis dri dang mi rnams kyi ni rkang pa lag pa dus kyi drod rnams rang bzhin rim pa yis// sna'i rtse mo 'phyang bar gyur pa dang ni spyi bor lag pas bzung na de'i rang bzhin mtho / 
47b4(rgyud): pa dang / lag mthil gnyis su rgya skyegs dmar po rab tu byugs par gyur kyang dmar por mi 'gyur ba nyid dang // nyi ma kha dog gnag dang ri bong 'dzin pa yongs su gang bar gyur pa kha dog ser por mthong // 
47b5(rgyud): gcin dang lus po drang mor gyur na de'i nyin zhag nyin la 'chi bar nges se mi'i bdag po kye// lce 'og skud pa nag par 'gyur da ga du tsha ma wA nan du rtsa wang dbugs ni zla ba nyi mar bskyong dang de bzhin 'khur ba gnyis
47b6(rgyud): g.yo yin na mi'i bdag po kye// nu ma'i steng gnas 'char khung nyid du zhugs te gza' tshogs mtha' dag me stag dang bcas mthong ba dang // mgrin pa lus par bcas pa rengs shing sems med yan lag
47b7(rgyud): bskor ba rnams ni 'chi ltas mtshan nyid do// gang zhig skyed dang rab tu skye ba'i dus dang byis pa dang ni gzhon nu la sogs gzugs su byed// 'jig rten du ni slar yang sdud par byed pa de nyid dus kyi 'khor la can
47b8(rgyud): lo can ste nyims min// mtshan mo'i cha la zla ba nyi ma la sogs lha rnams 'byung ba dang bcas bcom ldan 'das des snad// gzhan yang nyin mo'i dus su skyed pa'i don du ma lus pa la ster bar byed pa rim
48a1(rgyud): !/ pa yis/ sgra la sogs pa drug pa rnams las su 'gyur zhing gzhan yang bya ba shes pa dbang po drug rnams dang // lo dang zla ba rnams dang phyogs dang nyin mtshan tshes dang zla ba nyi ma rnams
