48a7(rgyud): mkha'i yon tan rnams dang yid dang blo dang ngar 'dzin rnams// rags dang 'phra dang gzhan rnams yon tan rnam pa gsum du gyur pa'i yi ge thig le sogs dbye bas// rags pa dbang po rags pa'i rang
48a8(rgyud): bzhin nyid du 'gyur te phra mo phra mo'i sems su yang ni brjod// ye shes nyid ni ye shes sku ste rang bzhin mi 'gyur ba'i 'tsho bar gyur pa 'byung ba min// a la sogs pa stong pa lnga rnams rang bzhin mi
48b1(rgyud): 'gyur ba ste dpal gyi cha dang thig le sgra// dus dang sems dang blo rnams de bzhin rnam 'gyur yin te de yang dbyangs rnams rlung la sogs pas so// sde tshan yi ge rnams ni bcu pa sum 'gyur rags pa nyid skye

48b3(rgyud): las skyes pa de la za// rags dang phra dang gzhan dang gsum po 'di rnams mi rnams ma 'dus las su 'gyur ba ste// bdag nyid byed po las dang bral dang gzhan yang dbang phyug phyugs dag byed po yod zhes
48b4(rgyud): 'dod pa las rtabadag gam gzhan gyi byed pos mi byed rang bzhin rnam bral de ni lam med shes par bya ba'o// de phyir byed pa po yis srog chags rnams la bde dang sdug bsngal cung zad ster dang 'phrog pa
48b5(rgyud): men/ 'khor bar gang zhig gis ni sngon du las nyid rnam gsum byas pa'i 'bras bu rab tu ster bar 'gyur// rmongs pa rnams kyi blo 'dis ster dang 'phrog pa dang / ste skyed dang sdud par byed par 'dod pa ste/ 
48b6(rgyud): rang gi dbang pos lus la skyon dag ma mthong pa yis dpag med dag ba 'phrog par byed pa'o// 'dod pa dang ni bya ba'i nus pa dag dang shes pa'i nus pa 'gro ba rnams kyi rang yid gsum// dngos po snang ba/

60a1(rgyud): gter du rnal 'byor pa yis rig par bya ba'o// dbang ldan dang ni byang gi sa'i steng du nges par zhi ba dang ni rgyas par 'gyur ba'o// me dang shar gyi cha ru rab tu gsal bar gsad pa dang
60a2(rgyud): nges par dbye dang bskrad pa'o// bden bral dang ni lho'i phyogs su gsal bar rtag tu dbang dang dgug par bya ba kho na'o// rlung dang nub kyi phyogs su nges par rmongs pa dang ni rengs par 'gyur ro mi'i bdag po kya/

60a4(rgyud): brgyad gyur pa rnams kyi nang du rigs kyi dbang las de nyid rnams kyi mtshan ma rnams/ pad ma khor mo gri gug nyid dang ral gri mda' zhes pa dang rdo rje lcags kyu lcags sgeg sbrul/ gcig dang ga
60a5(rgyud): dang phyed dang khru gang mkha' dus mkha' mig mkha' me nam mkha' mtshams kyi sor mor 'gyur// rgya'i phyed dang cha drag pa dang nyi ma rnam par dbye bas bskor ba zabs dang kha khyer dang // kha khyer steng

60a7(rgyud): yang ni 'gyur te sa la phur bu brgyad kyi dbye ba rnams// n+ya gre ta dang aM sha tha dang rus pa lcags dang seng ldeng um la a rga bi la skyes// 'di ltar dum pa rnams ni shel dang mchog gi rdul las byung dang

60b4(rgyud): ldeng skyes dang kyin shu ka dag dbang dang dgug pa la// bil ba dang ni bsko bad 'khrug byed pa nyid mda' brgya'i grangs rnams rengs dang rmongs par byed pa la// 'o ma mar dang khrag dang zhag dang dngul dang rdo//

60b8(rgyud): rigs kyi dbang las rdul tshon bri bar bya ba phyogs rnams su// bkod pa dang ni bsang gtor la sogs rang gi snying kha'i rdo rje nyid las lha rnams spro bar ba// shel la sogs pa yon chab snod rnams pad ma
61a1(rgyud): non gyi 'dab ma 'the ba so bcu gnyis pa nyid do// yu ba snyim pa dang ldan dgang gser nyid dang skyer mo can gyi blugs gsar dag gis sprin sreg pa// zhi dang drag dang chags bcas
61a2(rgyud): 'gyur te rigs kyi dbang las la rnams bsgyings pa'i sku nyid kha dog dag/ de ltar las ni gnyis su 'gyur te rab tu gsal bar nges par dkyil 'khor gyi ni lhag pa'i lha// rgyal ba'i dbang pos rna/

61b7(rgyud): par gyur pas sdig spangs pa ru rnal 'byor pa yis bsgom par bya ba'o// sa phyogs rnams su rdo rje gsum gyis dang po kho nar zhing skyong rnams la gtor ma sbyin byas la// phyis nas rdo rje bzhi rnams kyis
61b8(rgyud): ni phyogs mtshams gyur par gnas pa'i bdud kyi sde rnams nges par sreg/ sa yi lha mo sman drangs pa la chu bcas me tog yon tshab rnams ni 'di la rab tu sbyin// phyis nas sa stengs ji ltar 'dod pa
62a1(rgyud): sprin du spang bar bya phyir de la gsol ba gdab dang bstod pa bya// lha'i bdag po dang bcas bdud sde rgyal bas bcom dus lha mo khyod ni dbang du gyur pa'i tshe// khyod la lha'i mchog gis
62a2(rgyud): mched dang phyag byas bzhes pa'i phyir na de bzhin nga'i yon chab 'di'ang ba zhes// byang chub rgyu ru stobs mchog ldan pa'i bdud kyi sde rnams rgyal bas bcom pa ji lta ba bzhin du// de bzhin bdag kyang sleb
62a3(rgyud): ma rnams kyis dbang gis don du bdud kyi stobs rnams 'jigs par byed pa'o// sangs rgyas rnams dang sdig pa bral ba'i byang chub sems dpa' phyogs rnams la bzhugs gang dag btsun mor bcas//

62a5(rgyud): bcu'i khro bo mtshon cha ldan pa rnams ni phyogs kyi char gyur rnams la bsrung ba'i don du bgod// sa'i nang du rus pa sol bar bcas pa'i rwa rnams gsod 'jigs byed pa nges par yod pa na// de phyir gnas

62b1(rgyud): rigs kyi mtshan mo gzhan la rab gnas min// dus sbyor rnams dang gza' sogs bdag ni mtshan mo gzhan nyid la yang rab tu gnas par 'gyur ba ste/ srog dang pa ba sangs dag rgas nas med par gyur na ngags

63a1(rgyud): thabs kyi yan lag dbus kyi yongs su 'joms 'gom dkyil 'khor du ni spang bar bya ba yin// g.yul gyi dus su med dang rlung du gyur par sde'i dbus su sa la gdengs ka bzhin du'o//

63b1(rgyud): gyi bang la nyi byed rnams kyis rdul chen gnas su 'gyur ba ste// phyogs mtshams rnams su rgya mtsho re dmig rnams dang nyi ma'i ri mig pad ma rnams la dri sogs lha// phyed bcas gcig gis ri mo gsum du 'gyur te/

64a1(rgyud): tshon gyis de bzhin nyid// phyogs kyi cha'i rdul tshon gnas su sangs rgyas dbye bas rdul chen dgye bar bya'o mi'i bdag po kye// ser po dkar po dmar po la sogs rnams kyis sa

64b2(rgyud): kyi padan ni rlung la sogs par rab tu 'gyur// sa yi dkyil 'khor gyur pa'i dbang ldan dang ni srin po'i mtshams su zla ba nyi ma'i bdag po kye/ phyi rol sgos stengs cha ru chos kyi 'khor lo smin mtshungs ri ngag

64b4(rgyud): doshal byed pa kha dog dkar po 'gyur ste rigs kyi dbang las shing rta sgo'i dbus su'o// sgo'i phyi ru rlung gnas 'khor lo dkar po dang ni dmar po rang gi rgyal ba'i rigs dbang las// phyi ru rdo rje'i phreng ba rdo rje
64b5(rgyud): 'bar ba 'phro ba rnams su 'gyur ro mi yi bdag po kye// sbom pos nad byed pa dang re gang na dang 'phra bas rdzas rnams bri bar rab tu gsal bar 'gyur// chad pas 'chi ba dang ni 'khyog pos mi'i bdag po skye bor

65a1(rgyud): bram mams mas kyim rab tu 'ardzun// nag pa la thos rkang pas 'phes par 'gyur te tshan gyi sangs ni sa pa nas cig tsud du// rtsig pa rnams kyisam 'gyur bang pa'i bya
65a2(rgyud): phreng ba ruHsnying po nas ni sgo lasags pa'i mtshams su nor ldan 'gyur te dkyil 'khor 'jig rten khams nyid do// sgo rnams nas ni sur rtsi ka mtha'i rjengs ka gsum 'gyur bsregs pa rin chen
65a3(rgyud): kyi dkyil 'khor nyid// de yi phyi rol rgyal ba'i dbang po'i re dmyig rnams kyis me'i dkyil 'khor de nas rlung yang de ltar 'gyur// de'i phyi rol nyid du de'i rnam par dag pas sa chu'i byin pa rlung rnams bas/ 
65a4(rgyud): pa ru ni bya/ spyi gtsug zhal dang mgrin la gdengs ka sum 'gyur ba srogs pa rnams kyi dkyil 'khor gyis ni sbyang bar bya/ de ltar lhun po mtha' dag la ni gdengs ka sum 'gyur ba sregs pa rnas

94a1(rgyud): / ma las ni stag gdong ma yin rigs kyi dbang las ser mo 'bar las lce smang gdong // de ltar sgeg mo la sogs lha ma thams cad rnam pa chur gsal te yang sna tshogs yul

94a3(rgyud): rnal 'byor ma rnams longs spyod sku ste shing rta la gnas dang nyi ma lta bu rab tu grug/ klu brgyad rab tu se ma rnams 'khor gyi skye bo dang bcas rnams ni sangs rgyas rnams kyi sprul pa'i sku// de lta
94a4(rgyud): slar yang rgyal ba'i sku ni phyi dang nan du dbye ba rnam pa gnyis su 'gyur ba ni/ mngal du skye ba ji lta ba bzhin nges par nga rgyal 'khor du yang rab tu 'gyur ba'o// ston po lha mo la sogs bum po rnams

94b1(rgyud): pa'i sku dag zung du 'gyur// sems can rnams la thar pa sten pas yed shes dang ni sprul pa'i sku dag zung du nges par 'gyur/ shes rab thabs kyis lus dang bsam pa mnyam dang po mnyam rigs kyis

132a3(rgyud): ba'i gzugs ni nam mkhar nyin mo min ste mtshan mo nyid kyang cung zad min// thun mtshams de ni rnal 'byor pa rnams lus kyi dbugs su dus rnams kun tu bdud rtsi'i gnas gyur pa// zla ba phyed
132a4(rgyud): pa zad pa'i nam mkha' la gnas nyi ma bzhin du lus nyid ro mnyam 'gyur ba'o// lus la srog dang thur rgyu nges par zad de 'gags pa'i dus gsal ba grub par brjod pa'o// lam gnyis srog
